bba	Tem dɑɑ wɑ̃ɑwɑ bitɑm. Gɑ̃ɑnu kun wɑ̃ɑ mɛ sɔɔ.
bba	Mɛn temɔ wɔru bɔkɔwɑ ɡɑ wɑ̃ɑ mi, mɑ yɑm wɔ̃kurɑ
bba	ɡu wukiri. Mɑ nim mu tɛrie tem mɛn wɔllu ɡiɑ. Nim mɛn
bba	wɔllɔwɑ Gusunɔn Hunde rɑ n bɛllimɔ.
bba	Yen sɔ̃nɑ durɔ u koo win tundo kɑ win mɛro deri kpɑ wi
bba	kɑ win kurɔ bɑ n mɑninɛ, kpɑ be yiru kpuro bu ko wɑsi tee.
bba	nɑ tem bɔ̃rusi wunɛn sɔ̃.

bba	Adɑmɑ wunɛ Nɔwɛ, ɑ tii kpɑkoro bɑkɑru kuo kɑ dɑ̃ɑ
bba	dɑmɡiɑ, tɑ n dii sɔsu mɔ, kpɑ ɑ tu dɑ̃ɑ fĩifĩinu
bba	tɛɛni ten sɔɔwɔ kɑ tɔɔwɔ.
bba	Adɑmɑ Gusunɔ kun Nɔwɛ duɑri kɑ ɡbeeku yɛɛ kpuro kɑ
bba	yɑɑ sɑbe ni kpuro yi yi kɑ nùn wɑ̃ɑ kpɑkoro te sɔɔ.

bba	U Aburɑmu domɑru kuɑ u nɛɛ, Gusunɔ, wi, wi u kpuro kere, u

bba	Mɑ Sɑɑrɑi u Aburɑmu sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, nɛn wɔmburu tu
bba	wɔri wunɛ sɔɔ. Nɑ nun nɛn yoo kɑ̃ kurɔ, ɑdɑmɑ ye u
bba	wɑ mɑ u ɡurɑ mɔ, yerɑ u mɑn ɡɛndu wɔri. Yinni
bba	Gusunɔwɑ koo sun siriɑ nɛ kɑ wunɛ.
bba	Yerɑ u Gusunɔ sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, ɑ de Isimɛɛlin sɑnu

bba	Amɔnibɑn bweserɑ mɑɑ yɑrɑ.

bba	Adɑmɑ Eforoni u Aburɑhɑmu sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ,

bba	Isimɛɛlin bibun bweseru wee. Isimɛɛli u sɑ̃ɑwɑ
bba	Aburɑhɑmun bii wi u kɑ Aɡɑɑ Eɡibitiɡii mɑrɑ. Aɡɑɑ
bba	wi, u sɑ̃ɑwɑ Sɑɑrɑɑn yoo wi u Aburɑhɑmu wɛ̃ kurɔ.
bba	Gɔ̃ɔrɑ kpɑm duɑ tem mɛ sɔɔ, nɡe mɛ tɑ rɑɑ kuɑ
bba	Aburɑhɑmun wɑɑti. Mɑ Isɑki u dɑ u wɑ̃ɑ Abimɛlɛki
bba	Filisitibɑn sinɑ bokon mi Gerɑɔ.
bba	Ǹ n mɛn nɑ, ɑ bɔ̃ruo mɑ ɑ ǹ kɑɑ sun kɔ̃sɑ ɡɑɑ
bba	kuɑ nɡe mɛ sɑ nun ɡeɑ kuɑ sɑ derɑ ɑ doonɑ kɑ bɔri
bba	yɛndu bɛsɛn min di. Wee tɛ̃ Yinni Gusunɔ u nun domɑru
bba	Yɑkɔbu u susi win bɑɑbɑ Isɑkin mi, mɑ u nùn bɑbɑ u
bba	nɛɛ, Yɑkɔbun nɔɔwɑ nɑ nɔɔmɔ, ɑdɑmɑ Esɑun nɔmɑ
bba	Kɑɑ mɑɑ ko wunɛn wɔnɔn yoo.
bba	Ye u Hɑrɑni turuku tiɑ, yerɑ u mɛɛrɑ u dɔkɔ ɡɑɑ wɑ

bba	Mɑ Yɑkɔbu u kɑ nùn duɑ dɔmɑ te.
bba	Mɛyɑ Yɑkɔbu u kuɑ u kɑ dukiɑ wɑ yɑ kpɑ̃. U yɑ̃ɑnu

bba	ɡeu mɛɛri, wi, wi u sɑ̃ɑ nɛn tɔnwero.

bba	ten diyɑ u killimɔ kɑ ɡɑ̃ɑ te.
bba	6-7 Ye bɑ ɡɑri yi nuɑ, mɑ be kpuro bɑ mɔru bɛsirɑ ye
bba	Sikɛmu u kɑ Isirelin bweserun yĩsiru sɑnkɑ u kɑ ben sesu
bba	Dinɑ kpunɑ. Domi n ǹ weenɛ bu yen bweseru ko ben suunu
bba	Yɑkɔbu u tunumɑ, wi kɑ win tɔn be, Lusiɔ ye bɑ mɑɑ
bba	sokumɔ Betɛli, Kɑnɑnin temɔ.
bba	Mɑ Esɑu u dɑ u wɑ̃ɑ Seirin ɡuunun berɑ ɡiɑ. Esɑu

bba	Domi bɑ mɑn ɡbɛnɑwɑ sɑɑ Heberubɑn tem di, bɑ kɑ mɑn
bba	nɑ mini. Yen biru nɑ ǹ mɑɑ ɡɑ̃ɑnu kue bɑ kɑ mɑn
bba	Mɑ doo winu nɔɔbɑ yiru ɡɑnu nu mɑɑ yɑrɑ niɔnɔn temɔ
bba	ni nu sɑkosu sɑ̃ɑ nu ɡbere sɔ̃ɔ kɑ woon sɔ̃.

bba	Mɑ ben bɑɑwure u win sɑɑki yi temɔ kɑ sɛndɑru u kusiɑ.

bba	Be bɑ sɑ̃ɑ Yɑkɔbun bweseru be bɑ nɑ Eɡibitiɔ, ben
bba	Bɑ nùn wisɑ bɑ nɛɛ, yɑɑ sɑbenɑ sɑ rɑ kpɑre, yinni.
bba	Mɛyɑ mɑɑ bɛsɛn bɑɑbɑbɑn tii.

bba	ye n koo bɛɛ deemɑ ɑmɛn biru.

bba	Ye Mɔwisi u nɑ u di mɑ u wurɑ u kɑ sinɑ durɔ win mi. Mɑ
bba	u nùn bii ben turo kɑ̃ kurɔ, wi bɑ mɔ̀ Seforɑ.
bba	Mɑ Mɔwisi kɑ Aroni bɑ ɡurenɑ bɑ dɑ Eɡibitiɔ, bɑ

bba	Eɡibitiɡibɑ bu koosiɑmɔn di. Kon bu yɑkiɑ ben yorun di,

bba	Eɡibiti sunɔ u ǹ Mɔwisi kɑ Aronin ɡɑri swɑɑ dɑki.
bba	Yinni Gusunɔ u derɑ win ɡɔ̃ru ɡɑ bɔbiɑ ɡɑ sosi nɡe
bba	Mɑ bɑ derɑ Mɔwisi kɑ Aroni bɑ wurɑmɑ Eɡibiti sunɔn mi.
bba	Ye bɑ turɑ mi, yerɑ u bu sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, i doo i Gusunɔ
bba	bɛɛn Yinni sɑ̃, ɑdɑmɑ bɛɛ sɔɔ berɑ̀ bɑ koo dɑ.
bba	Ye u ɡɑri yi ɡeruɑ u kpɑ, mɑ u yɑrɑ Eɡibiti sunɔn min

bba	seeyɑtiɑ doke. Yen nɔɔbɑ yirusen tii sɔɔrɑ i ko Yinni
bba	Gusunɔ tɔ̃ɔ bɑkɑru diiyɑ.
bba	I yɔ̃ro sɛ̃ɛ, Yinni Gusunɔwɑ u koo bɛɛ sɑnnɑ.
bba	Bɛrum kɑ nɑndɑbu koo bu deemɑ subɑru sɔɔ.
bba	Mɑ Yinni Gusunɔ u Mɔwisi sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ,

bba	tɔn beni kuɑ. Wee, bɑ kĩ bu mɑn kpenu kɑsuku.
bba	Tɛ̃ ɑ nɛn ɡɑri nɔɔwɔ, kpɑ Gusunɔ u nun somi. Bwisi yi
bba	kon nun kɛ̃ wee. A koowo tɔn ben wiruɡii Gusunɔn
bba	wuswɑɑɔ, kpɑ ɑ n dɑ kɑ ben ɡɑri de win mi.

bba	mɑn mɛɛri, kpɑ ben dɑbiru tu ku rɑɑ kɑm ko.

bba	Ye kon mɑɑ wure n ko wee. Be bɑ nuɑ i duɔ ben temɔ kpuro,
bba	kon de bu nɑndɑ, kpɑ bu yɑri bu doonɑ bɛɛn sɔ̃.

bba	Yinni Gusunɔ u Mɔwisi sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, ɑ bekunu wɔkuru
bba	wesio kɑ wɛ̃ɛ dɑmɡii kɑ wɛ̃ɛ yi bɑ wɔ̃kuɑ kɑ

bba	weenɑsibu. Kpɑ ɑ kɑ mɑn kuu bekuruɡiru kuɑ.
bba	À n beku kɑre te bwɛ̃ ɑ kpɑ, ten sɔɔwɔwɑ kɑɑ kɑ
bba	kpɑkoro te dɑ ɑ yi tè sɔɔ woodɑn kpee bɛsi yiru ye, yɑ
bba	wɑ̃ɑ. Kpɑ ɑ kpɑkoro te wukiritiɑ dokeɑ dii te tɑ

bba	tɑrɑkpe ɡe. Kpɑ yɑ n yinusi ɡe sɔɔ.

bba	sɛ̃kɑtiɑ ye bɑ sɔmɑ doke.
bba	Yen biru kpɑ ɑ ye kpuro mwɑ ben nɔmɑn di ɑ ye sɔndi
bba	yɑ̃ku dɔ̃ɔ mwɑɑrɑ ten wɔllɔ kpɑ ɑ dɔ̃ɔ doke kpɑ
bba	yɑ n sɑ̃ɑ yɑ̃ku dɔ̃ɔ mwɑɑrɑruɡii te tɑ mɑn nuburu
bba	Yinni Gusunɔ u kpɑm Mɔwisi sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ,
bba	Kɑ nɡe mɛ bɑ rɑ kpee ɡobiɡinu sɔɔ yore ni bɑ koo
bba	ɡore, kɑ sere mɑɑ dɑ̃ɑ dɑ̃kubu, ye kpuro ɡesi ye n
bba	Ye bɑ sɑrɑm wee, Yosue u tɔmbun wurenu nuɑ nɡe mɛ bɑ
bba	ɡbisimɔ. U Mɔwisi sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, tɑbun wurenu wɑ̃ɑ
bba	Mɔwisi u Yinni Gusunɔ sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, wee, ɑ nɛɛ, n kɑ
bba	tɔn be doo tem mɛ sɔɔ. Mɛyɑ ɑ mɑɑ nɛɛ, ɑ mɑn yɛ̃
bba	sɑ̃ɑ sɑ̃ɑ. Kɑɑ n kɑ mɑn nɔnu ɡeu mɛɛrɑ. Adɑmɑ
bba	ɑ ǹ mɑn sɔ̃ɔwɑ wi u koo mɑn yɔ̃siri.
bba	Ǹ n kɛtɛkun nɑ, i kɑ ɡen buu ɡbiikuu yɑ̃ɑ buu
bba	kɔsinɔ kpɑ ɡu ko yɑ̃ku yɑ̃ɑru. Ì kun mɑɑ kue mɛ, i
bba	ɡen wĩi sumɑ buo i ɡo. I ko bii ɡbiikoo tɔn durɔ
bba	kɑ dɑbu ɡe, kɑ ɡen dendi yɑ̃nu kpuro, kɑ ɡen fitilɑnu,
bba	Yen biru bɑ bekɑ yen nɔɔbu suɑ bɑ swɛɛnɑ. Nɡe mɛyɑ
bba	bɑ mɑɑ kuɑ kɑ nɔɔbu ye yɑ tie.
bba	Mɑ u dɑ̃ɑ pɔɔsi kuɑ yiru u yi wurɑ pote.
bba	Mɑ bɑ dɑ̃ɑ pɔɔsi yi wɑsi sumi yi sɔɔ beri berikɑ yi
bba	bɑ ko n dɑ kɑ yɑ̃ku yee te sue. Bɑ tu kuɑwɑ kɑ dɑ̃ɑ
bba	Bɑ mɑɑ bɔɔ bɑrɑ ye kuɑ. Ye kɑ yɑbe tɑrɑkpe ɡe, yɑ
bba	sɑ̃ɑwɑ beku nɔni tee kɑ burɑ teeru.
bba	kɑ kpɑkoro wurɑɡiru tèn wɔllɔ bɑ ko n dɑ turɑre
bba	dɔ̃ɔ doke, kɑ ɡum mɛ bɑ ko n dɑ kpuro tɑ̃re bu kɑ
bba	sɔ̃ɔsi mɑ Gusunɔ u ye ɡɔsɑ nɛnɛm, kɑ turɑre nubu
bba	Mɑ u pɛ̃ɛ ye yoruɑ tɑbulu wɔllɔ mɑm mɑm, ye bɑ kɑ
bba	Yinni Gusunɔ nɑɑwɑ, nɡe mɛ u nùn sɔ̃ɔwɑ.
bba	U koo ɡen sɑnsu wukiriwɑ kpɑ u ɡen yɔ̃ɔru wĩɑ u kɔ̃
bba	yɑ̃ku yerun sɔ̃ɔ yɑri yeru ɡiɑ mì bɑ rɑ torom wisi.
bba	Wee ye bɑ koo Yinni Gusunɔ dɔ̃ɔ dokeɑ, yerɑ ɡum mɛ mu
bba	Adɑmɑ ù n tubɑ mɑ u torɑwɑ, boo niu ɡe ɡɑ ǹ ɑlebu
bba	ɡɑɑ mɔwɑ u koo kɑ yɑ̃kuru ko Gusunɔ u kɑ nùn win
bba	tɔnu win bweseru u Yinni Gusunɔ torɑriwɑ mi. U koo ɡɑ̃ɑ
bba	ni u ɡbɛnɑ mi wesiɑ, ǹ kun mɛ ni u kɑwɑ mi, ǹ kun mɛ
bba	ye bɑ nùn berusiɑ mi, ǹ kun mɛ ye u dɔbɑ mɑ u siki,
bba	Mi bɑ rɑ yɑ̃ku dɔ̃ɔ mwɑɑrɑruɡirun yɑɑ sɑke, miyɑ
bba	bɑ koo mɑɑ ten yɑɑ sɑkɑ, kpɑ bu yɑɑ yen yɛm yɛ̃kɑ
bba	yɑ̃ku yerun nɔɔ bɔkɑɔ bu kɑ sikerenɑ.
bba	Yɑ̃ku yɑɑ yen nɔmu nɔm ɡeuɡuu ɡɑ ko n mɑɑ sɑ̃ɑwɑ
bba	Mɑ u pɛ̃ɛ suɑ bireru sɔɔ ye bɑ ǹ seeyɑtiɑ doke kɑ
bba	kirɑ te bɑ kuɑ kɑ ɡum kɑ sere mɑɑ kirɑ sɔndɑnu. Mɑ u
bba	ye kpuro sɔndi yɑɑ ɡum mɛn wɔllɔ kɑ yɑ̃ɑ nɔmu ɡen
bba	Mɑ Aroni u yɑɑ yen ɡuro ɡuro ni suɑ kɑ yen nɔm ɡeu ɡe,
bba	u sɔ̃ɔsi beri berikɑ Yinni Gusunɔn wuswɑɑɔ nɡe mɛ
bba	Mɛyɑ bɑ ǹ koo mɑɑ wukun yɑɑ tem domi ɡɑ ǹ nɑɑ
bba	kɑburosu mɔ bɑɑ mɛ ɡɑ rɑ tukɑ ko. Bɑ koo ɡu
bba	Yɑɑ ye bɑ rɑ di yɑ̀ n kɑ tii ɡu, wi u yen ɡoru bɑbɑ,
bba	yɛ̃ro u disi duurɑwɑ mi sere n kɑ ko tɔ̃ɔ ten yokɑ.
bba	Adɑmɑ dɔmɑ te bɑ boo swɑ̃ɔ wɑ win wɑsi sɔɔ, bɑ koo
bba	Wi u bɑrɑ disiɡiru mɔ kpuro, u koo yɑ̃nu dokewɑ ni nu
bba	ɡɛ̃ɛre, u ku furɔ doke, kpɑ u win wuswɑɑ wukiri kpɑ u n
bba	nɔɔɡiru sue u n mɔ̀, disiɡii, disiɡii.
bba	Kpɑ u nùn torɑrun yɑ̃kuru kuɑ. Nɡe mɛyɑ u koo kɑ nùn
bba	dɛɛrɑsiɑ. Yen biruwɑ u koo yɑ̃ku dɔ̃ɔ
bba	U koo ɡunɔ ɡen teu sɑkɑwɑ wekeru sɔɔ te bɑ kuɑ kɑ
bba	Tɔn kurɔ wi u yɛm wĩimɔ, win yɑsɑn sɑɑ bɑɑsi, ǹ kun
bba	mɛ, mu wĩimɔ mu win yɑsɑn sɑɑ kerɑ, bɑ koo nùn
bba	ɡɑrisiwɑ disiɡii yɛm wĩi bin sɑɑ kpuro sɔɔ nɡe win
bba	Yen biru u koo wurɑ kuu ten mi, kpɑ u win sɑ̃ɑ yɑ̃ɑ ni u
bba	I ku rɑ ko ye bɑ rɑ ko Eɡibitiɔ mi i rɑɑ sinɑ. I ku
bba	mɑɑ ko ye Kɑnɑnibɑ mɔ̀ mi nɑ kɑ bɛɛ dɔɔ. I ku ben
bba	I ku tii bũnu wɛ̃, i ku rɑ mɑɑ bwɑ̃ɑroku ɡɑɡu seku.
bba	I de bɛɛn kilobɑ kɑ bɛɛn sɑkɑkunu ye kpuro yɑ n sɑ̃ɑ
bba	dee dee. Nɛ Gusunɔ bɛɛn Yinniwɑ nɑ ye ɡeruɑ, nɛ wi nɑ
bba	I de i n dɛɛre i n wɑ̃ɑ nɛn sɔ̃, domi nɑ dɛɛre. Nɛ,
bba	Yinni Gusunɔwɑ nɑ bɛɛ wunɑ nɛnɛm bwese ni nu tien suunu
bba	sɔɔn di i n kɑ sɑ̃ɑ nɛɡibu.
bba	Wi u yen ɡɑɑ bɑbɑ ɡesi, u disi duurɑwɑ mi sere kɑ
bba	yokɑɔ. U ǹ kpɛ̃ u yɑ̃ku dĩɑ ni di mɑ n kun mɔ u
bba	Yinni Gusunɔ u nɛɛ, wɔ̃ɔn suru ɡbiikoon sɔ̃ɔ wɔkurɑ
bba	nnɛsen yokɑn di, i Gɔɔ sɑrɑribun tɔ̃ɔ bɑkɑru dio nɛ,
bba	Suru nɔɔbɑ yirusen sɔ̃ɔ wɔkurɑ nɔɔbuse sɔɔ, ì n
bba	bɛɛn ɡberun dĩɑnu ɡɑ̃, i ko i tɔ̃ɔ bɑkɑru diwɑ
bba	sɔ̃ɔ nɔɔbɑ yiru i kɑ mɑn bɛɛrɛ wɛ̃. Yen tɔ̃ɔ
bba	ɡbiikiru kɑ yen tɔ̃ru nɔɔbɑ itɑse, i ko i wɛ̃rɑwɑ i
bba	Bɑɑ dĩɑ ni nu wɔrumɑ sɑnɑm mɛ i ɡɛ̃ɛmɔ mɑ nu
bba	kpiɑ kɑ tii, i ǹ nu ɡɛ̃ɛmɔ. I ǹ mɑɑ resɛm sɔrimɔ
bba	ye yɑ kɑ tii mɑrɑ. Domi bɛɛn ɡbeɑ yɑ koo wɛ̃rɑwɑ
bba	À n nùn ɡɑ̃ɑnu bɔkurɑ, ɑ ku nùn ɑre kɑsusi. A de ɑ
bba	nɛ Gusunɔ wunɛn Yinni nɑsiɑ, kpɑ wunɛn winsim u wɑ u n
bba	Nɑ kon sĩimɔwɑ bɛɛn suunu sɔɔ kpɑ nɑ n sɑ̃ɑ bɛɛn
bba	Yinni kpɑ i n mɑɑ sɑ̃ɑ nɛn tɔmbu.
bba	Ben biru, tem mɛ, mu koo wɛ̃rɑ. Sɑɑ ye sɔɔrɑ bɑ koo
bba	sɛɛyɑsiɑbu wɑ yèn sɔ̃ bɑ nɛn woodɑbɑ deri.
bba	Gɑ̃ɑ ni bɑ Yinni Gusunɔ kɑ̃ sere kɑ bɑɑdommɑɔ, ɑɑ
bba	tɔnuwɑ? Ǹ kun mɛ yɑɑ sɑberɑ? Ǹ kun mɛ ɡbee te u
bba	tubi diwɑ? Gɑ̃ɑ ni bɑ ɡɔsɑ bɑ yi Yinni Gusunɔn sɔ̃
bba	ɡesi, n ǹ mɑɑ koorɔ u nu yɑkiɑ ǹ kun mɛ u nu dɔrɑ.
bba	Nu ko n sɑ̃ɑwɑ Yinni Gusunɔɡinu sere kɑ bɑɑdommɑɔ.
bba	Gɑdin bweseru sɔɔ, bɑ sɑ̃ɑwɑ tɔmbu nɔrɔbun subɑ
bba	weeru kɑ nɔɔbu kɑ nɑtɑ kɑ weerɑɑkuru (45.650).
bba	Isirelibɑ bɑ̀ n sɑnum seewɑ, berɑ bɑ ko n dɑ ɡbi.
bba	Bɑǹ Lefibɑn bweseru ɡɑrɑ yèn sɔ̃ Yinni Gusunɔ u
bba	Mɔwisi sɔ̃ɔwɑ u ku bu ɡɑri.
bba	Ben kpɑron yĩsirɑ Elisɑfɑni, Usiɛlin bii.
bba	Bɑ koo dɑbu ɡe, kɑ ɡen dendi yɑ̃ɑ ni kpuro dokewɑ
bba	bɔɔru sɔɔ te bɑ kuɑ kɑ ɡɔni dɑmɡiɑ. Yen biru, kpɑ
bba	bu tu sɑ̃ɑrusiɑ dɑ̃ɑ pɔturɑ sɔɔ ye bɑ koo kɑ tu
bba	Mɑ Isirelibɑ bɑ Yinni Gusunɔn woodɑ ye mɛm nɔɔwɑ. Mɑ
bba	bɑ tɔmbu kpuro yɑrɑ be bɑ disi mɔ mi, nɡe mɛ Yinni
bba	Sɑɑ ye u tii Gusunɔ wɛ̃ mi, uǹ ɡɑ̃ɑnu dimɔ ye bɑ
bba	Yinni Gusunɔ u Mɔwisi sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ,
bba	kɑ kɛtɛ kinɛnu yɛndɑ nnɛ, kɑ yɑ̃ɑ kinɛnu wɑtɑ kɑ
bba	boo kinɛnu wɑtɑ kɑ yɑ̃ɑ kpɛmminu wɔ̃ɔ tiɑɡinu
bba	wɑtɑ. Ni kpurowɑ bɑ koo kɑ siɑrɑbun yɑ̃kunu ko. Kɛ̃ɛ
bba	niniwɑ bɑ kuɑ sɑnɑm mɛ bɑ yɑ̃ku yee te ɡum yɛ̃kɑ
bba	tɑ n kɑ sɑ̃ɑ nɛnɛm Gusunɔn sɔ̃.
bba	Mɑ Mɔwisi u Isirelibɑ sɔ̃ɔwɑ nɡe mɛ bɑ koo kɑ Gɔɔ
bba	sɑrɑribun tɔ̃ɔ bɑkɑru di.
bba	Mɑ Isirelibɑ bɑ seewɑ Sinɑin ɡbɑburun di bɑ swɑɑ wɔri
bba	nɡe mɛ bɑ woodɑ yi bu kɑ swĩinɑ. Mɑ ɡuru wii wuro te,
bba	Yinni Gusunɔ u Mɔwisi sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, ɑ mɑn Isirelibɑn
bba	ɡuro ɡurobu wɑtɑ kɑ wɔku te tɑ sɑ̃ɑ wiruɡibu
bba	mɛnnɑmɑ. A de bu nɑ nɛn kuu ten mi kɑ wunɛ sɑnnu.
bba	Yerɑ ɡuru wii wuro te, tɑ doonɑ. Mɑ Gusunɔ u derɑ bɑrɑ
bba	disiɡirɑ Mɑriɑmu wɔri u bɑu kpikisu yɑrɑ nɡe wɛ̃su.
bba	Mɑ Aroni u Mɑriɑmu mɛɛrɑ u deemɑ bɑrɑ disiɡirɑ tɑ
bba	Mɑ bɑ tunumɑ wɔwɑ ye bɑ mɔ̀ Ɛsikoliɔ. Miyɑ bɑ resɛm
bba	kɑ̃ɑsɑ burɑ kɑ sere yen swɑɑru. Mɑ bɑ ye sɔɔwɑ be
bba	yiru bɑ sɑ̃ɑrusie kɑ dɛkɑ. Bɑ mɑɑ dɑ̃ɑ mɑrum ɡɑm
bba	suɑ mɛ bɑ mɔ̀ ɡerenɑdi kɑ fiɡi.
bba	Adɑmɑ sere kɑ nɛn wɑ̃ɑru kɑ sere mɑɑ nɛn yiiko ye yɑ
bba	Ǹ n mɑɑ kɛtɛn nɑ, bɑ kɑ yɑ̃ku dɔ̃ɔ
bba	mwɑɑrɑruɡiru mɔ̀, ǹ kun mɛ siɑrɑbun yɑ̃kuru, ǹ
bba	kun mɛ nɔɔ mwɛɛrun yɑ̃kuru, ǹ kun mɛ yɑ̃kuru ɡɑru,
bba	Nɡe mɛyɑ bɑ koo kɑ nɛn woodɑbɑ yɑɑyɑ, kpɑ bu kɑ ye
bba	mɛm nɔɔwɑ kpɑ bɑ n sɑ̃ɑ nɛnɛm nɛn sɔ̃.
bba	Mɑ Mɔwisi u nɛɛ, tɛ̃ i ko i ɡiɑ mɑ Gusunɔwɑ u mɑn
bba	ɡɔsɑ n kɑ sɔmɑ ye ko ye i wɑɑmɔ nɑ mɔ̀. Nɑǹ ye
bba	Bururu yɑm sɑ̃reru Mɔwisi u duɑ kuru mi, mɑ u deemɑ
bba	Aronin dɛkɑ ye yɑ sɑ̃ɑ Lefibɑn dɛkɑ, yɑ kpɑrɑ yɑ
bba	wɛ̃su kuɑ sere yɑ binu mɑrɑ nu ye.
bba	Nɡe mɛyɑ ben tii bɑ koo mɑɑ kɑ ben kɛ̃nu nɑ ni nu
bba	sɑ̃ɑ nɡe ben ɡberun dĩɑnu, ǹ kun mɛ tɑm.
bba	Mbɑn sɔ̃nɑ ɑ kɑ bɛsɛ Gusunɔn tɔmbu nɑ ɡbɑburu sɔɔ
bba	mini su kɑ ɡbi bɛsɛ kɑ bɛsɛn yɑɑ sɑbenu.
bba	Yerɑ Yinni Gusunɔ u bu wɛɛ dɛ̃ɛɡii sure mɑ ben dɑbirɑ
bba	kɑ bũu ni nu wɑ̃ɑ Aɑnɔɔn ɡunɡunu wɔllɔ.
bba	Domi u koo be nun bɛɛrɛ bɑkɑ wɛ̃. U koo ko kpuro ye ɑ
bba	nùn bikiɑ. A ɡesi nɑ ɑ nùn tɔn be bɔ̃rusiɑ.
bba	Yerɑ Yinni Gusunɔ u nùn kure mɑ Bɑlɑmu u ɡeruɑ u nɛɛ,
bba	wee nɑ yɑ̃ku yenu nɔɔbɑ yiru kuɑ mɑ nɑ kɛtɛ kɑ
bba	yɑ̃ɑru ɡo yɑ̃ku yee nin bɑɑteren wɔllɔ.
bba	Wee Gusunɔ u mɑn woodɑ wɛ̃ n Isirelibɑ domɑru kuɑ.
bba	Mɑ nu ɡire nɡe dɑ̃ɑ ni bɑ mɔ̀ sɛduru ni Yinni Gusunɔ
bba	Mɑ u kɑ win sinɑ dɛkɑ Mɔɑbubɑ soomɔ bɑɑ sɑburosɔ.
bba	Yen sɔ̃, ɑ nùn sɔ̃ɔwɔ ɑ nɛɛ, wee nɑ kɑ nùn
bba	ɑrukɑwɑni bɔkumɔ ye yɑ sɑ̃ɑ bɔri yɛnduɡiɑ.
bba	Be bɑ sɑ̃ɑ Sɑbulonin bwese kɛri toruɑ, berɑ mi. Ben
bba	ɡeerɑ sɑ̃ɑwɑ tɔmbu nɔrɔbun subɑ wɑtɑ kɑ nɛɛrɑ
bba	Be bɑ sɑ̃ɑ Lefin bwese kɛri, berɑ Libinɑn yɛnuɡibu, kɑ
bba	Heboronin yɛnuɡibu kɑ Mɑkirin yɛnuɡibu, kɑ Musin
bba	yɛnuɡibu, kɑ Koren yɛnuɡibu, Kehɑtiwɑ u Amurɑmu mɑrɑ.
bba	ɑ Isirelibɑ woodɑ yeni wɛ̃ɛyɔ.
bba	Suru nɔɔbɑ yirusen tɔ̃ɔ ɡbiikiru sɔɔ, i ku sɔmburu
bba	ɡɑru ko. I ko i mɛnnɑwɑ i Yinni Gusunɔ tɑkɑru ko. I ko i
bba	tɔ̃ɔ te diwɑ i n kɔbi soomɔ.
bba	Bii wɔndiɑ ù n Yinni Gusunɔ nɔɔ mwɛɛru kuɑ, ǹ kun
bba	mɛ, ù n bɔ̃ruɑ sɑnɑm mɛ u ɡinɑ wɑ̃ɑ win tundon
bba	Adɑmɑ i tii wɔndiɑbɑ yiiyo be bɑǹ durɔ yɛ̃.
bba	Yen sɔ̃nɑ sɑ kɑ Yinni Gusunɔ tɑkɑrun kɛ̃nu nɑɑwɑ ni
bba	bɑ kuɑ kɑ wurɑ. Niyɑ sumi kɑ tɑɑminu kɑ swɑɑ tonkunu
bba	kɑ yɔni. Kpɑ nu n sɑ̃ɑ nɡe torɑrun yɑ̃kuru.
bba	Kpɑ bɛsɛ kpuro su Yuudɛni tɔburɑ sɑ n tɑbu yɑ̃nu nɛni
bba	su kɑ tɑbu ko Yinni Gusunɔn wuswɑɑɔ nɡe mɛ ɑ ɡeruɑ.
bba	Sɑɑ min diyɑ bɑ dɑ bɑ ben sɑnsɑni ɡirɑ Hɑserɔtuɔ.
bba	Mɑ bɑ ben sɑnsɑni ɡirɑ mi, sɑɑ Bɛti Yɛsimɔtin di, n
bba	Kɑ Elisɑfɑni, Pɑɑnɑkin bii, Sɑbulonin bweseru sɔɔ,
bba	Bu ku nɔm birɑn kɛ̃ru mwɑ bu kɑ tɔn ɡowo deri. N weenɛ
bba	Mɑ nɑ wiruɡii be woodɑ wɛ̃ nɑ nɛɛ, ben mɛro bisibu
bba	bɑ̀ n ɡɑri mɔ ben tii tiinɛ sɔɔ, ǹ kun mɛ, kɑ tɔn
bba	tuko, bu bu swɑɑ dɑkio kpɑ bu bu siriɑ dee dee.
bba	Yen biru mɑ sɑ ɡɔsirɑ sɑ dɑ kɑ ɡbɑburun swɑɑ nim
bba	wɔ̃ku ɡe bɑ mɔ̀ Nɑɑ yɑrin berɑ ɡiɑ nɡe mɛ Yinni
bba	Gusunɔ u ɡeruɑ. Mɑ sɑ sirenɑ Seirin ɡuunɔ n kɑ tɛ.
bba	Mɑ Sihoni kɑ win tɑbu kowobu bɑ nɑ bɑ sun tɑbu wɔri
bba	Adɑmɑ Yinni Gusunɔ u kɑ mɑn mɔru kuɑ bɛɛn sɔ̃ mɑ u
bba	yinɑ u nɛn kɑnɑru nɔ. U nɛɛ, yɑ turɑ mɛ. N ku mɑɑ
bba	Miyɑ i ko i bũnu sɑ̃ ni tɔmbɑ kuɑ kɑ dɑ̃ɑ ǹ kun mɛ
bba	kɑ kpenu ni nu ku rɑ yɑm wɑ, nu ku rɑ ɡɑri nɔ, nu ku rɑ
bba	Su ku rɑ wi, Gusunɔ bɛsɛn Yinnin yĩsiru soku kɑm. Domi wi
bba	u win yĩsiru sokɑ kɑm, u koo yɛ̃ro sɛɛyɑsiɑ.
bba	I ye yoruo bɛɛn diɑn ɡɑmbon kɑdiribɑ sɔɔ kɑ wuun duu
bba	Sɔrɔkudo i ko i ɡere bɛɛn ɡɔ̃ruɔ i nɛɛ, bwese ni, nu
bba	bɛɛ dɑm kere. Amɔnɑ i ko i ko i kɑ nu ɡirɑ.
bba	Wee i ko bu ɡirɑ. Gisɔ i ko i ɡiɑ mɑ Gusunɔ bɛsɛn
bba	Yinnin tiiwɑ u ko n bɛɛ ɡbiiye nɡe dɔ̃ɔ wi u rɑ kpuro
bba	kɑm koosie. U koo de bu yɑrinɑ bɛɛn wuswɑɑn di u bu
bba	kpeerɑsiɑ. I ko i bu ɡirɑ kpɑ i bu kɑm koosiɑ fuuku nɡe
bba	mɛ Yinni Gusunɔ u bɛɛ sɔ̃ɔwɑ.
bba	Yen biru, bɛsɛ Isirelibɑ sɑ doonɑ Beerɔtu Bɛnɛ Yɑkɑnin
bba	di sɑ dɑ Mɔserɑɔ. Miyɑ Aroni u kpunɑ u ɡu mɑ sɑ nùn
bba	sikɑ mi. Mɑ win bii Eleɑsɑɑ u kuɑ yɑ̃ku kowo win ɑyerɔ.
bba	U koo mɑɑ de yɑkɑsu su kpi bɛɛn yɑɑ sɑbenun sɔ̃. I ko
bba	Adɑmɑ i ko i nu kowɑ yɑm mi Yinni Gusunɔ u koo ɡɔsi
bba	bɛɛn bwese kɛri tiɑn temɔ kpɑ i ko mi kpuro ye nɑ bɛɛ
bba	Bɑ̀ n ye kuɑn nɑ, sɑɑ yerɑ i ko wuu ɡen tɔmbu kpuro ɡo
bba	kɑ ben yɑɑ sɑbenu kpɑ i wuu ɡen tii kpeerɑsiɑ kɑ ye yɑ
bba	kpɑ yɑ n sɑ̃ɑ Lefibɑɡiɑ be, be bɑ ǹ tem mɔ bɛɛn
bba	suunu sɔɔ kɑ sɔbuɡiɑ kɑ ɡobekubɑɡiɑ kɑ
bba	ɡɔminibuɡiɑ be bɑ wɑ̃ɑ bɛɛn suunu sɔɔ, kpɑ bu di bu
bba	debu kpɑ Gusunɔ bɛsɛn Yinni u bɛɛ domɑru kuɑ bɛɛn
bba	Sɑɑ yèn di i dĩɑnu ɡɛ̃ɛbu toruɑ, i ko i ɑlusumɑ
bba	ɡɑriwɑ yu kɑ ko nɔɔbɑ yiru.
bba	Tire te, tɑ ko n wɑ̃ɑwɑ win bɔkuɔ kpɑ u n dɑ tu ɡɑri
bba	tɔ̃ɔ bɑɑtere win wɑ̃ɑrun tɔ̃ru kpuro sɔɔ kpɑ u kɑ
bba	ɡiɑ nɡe mɛ u koo Gusunɔ win Yinni nɑsiɑ, u win woodɑbɑ
bba	kɑ win yiirebu mɛm nɔɔwɑ.
bba	Nɡe mɛyɑ bɑ ǹ koo mɑɑ be bɑ kun toren yɛm yɑri tem
bba	mɛ sɔɔ mɛ Gusunɔ bɛsɛn Yinni u bɛɛ wɛ̃ i n mɔ, kpɑ
bba	yɛ̃ron yɛm mu kun wɑ̃ɑ bɛɛn winɔ.
bba	Dɑ̃ɑ te i yɛ̃ tɑ ǹ sɑ̃ɑ diirɑru, terɑ i ko i kpĩ i
bba	burɑ i kɑ sɛri ko yi i ko i kɑ ɡbɑ̃rɑru yɔ sere i kɑ
bba	Ì n dii kpɑɑru bɑnɑ i kpɑ, i ten tɛɛrɑ wɔllɔ ɡɑni
bba	dumi dokeo i kɑ sikerenɑ kpɑ bɑɑ ɡoo ù n wɔrumɑ min di
bba	Ì n yɑrɑ i kɑ yibɛrɛbɑ tɑbu wɔri, sɑɑ ye sɔɔrɑ i
bba	ko i tii lɑɑkɑri ko kɑ ɡɑ̃ɑ disiɡinu kpuro.
bba	Bɑ ǹ tɔnu ɡoomɔ win biin torɑrun sɔ̃, mɛyɑ bɑ ǹ
bba	mɑɑ bii ɡoomɔ win mɔwɔbun torɑrun sɔ̃. Bɑ ǹ ɡoo
bba	Adɑmɑ Eɡibitiɡibu bɑ bu dɑm dɔre, bɑ bu nɔni
bba	sɔ̃ɔwɑ, mɑ bɑ bu kuɑ yobu.
bba	Kpɑ Lefibɑ bu nɛɛ, bɔ̃rurowɑ wi u win winsim tem nɔɔ
bba	burɑ yeru sɑre. Kpɑ tɔmbu kpuro bu nɛɛ, ɑmi!
bba	U koo de bɛɛn wɑsi yi ɡberɑ ǹ kun mɛ yi swĩɑ ǹ kun
bba	mɛ yi mɔsi ǹ kun mɛ yi wooru bɑrɑ. U koo mɑɑ yinɑ
bba	ɡurɑ yu nɛ kpɑ bɛɛn ɡbeɑn dĩɑnu nu ɡberɑ ǹ kun mɛ
bba	nu kɔ̃si. Wɑhɑlɑ ye kpurowɑ i ko wɑ sere u kɑ bɛɛ
bba	Sɑnɑm mɛ bɛɛn yibɛrɛ be, bɑ bɛɛ tɑrusi, ɡɔ̃ɔrɑ
bba	koo ko sere i bɛɛn bibu tem be Yinni Gusunɔ u bɛɛ wɛ̃.
bba	Yen sɔ̃, bɛɛn suunu sɔɔ, ɡoo ǹ kun mɛ yɛnu ɡɑɡu
bba	ǹ kun mɛ bwese kɛrɑ ɡɑɑ yu ku rɑɑ Gusunɔ bɛsɛn
bba	Yinni biru kisi kpɑ yu dɑ yu bwese tuku nin bũnu sɑ̃.
bba	Bɛɛn suunu sɔɔ, ɡoo u ku rɑɑ ɡɔsirɑ u ko nɡe dɑ̃ɑ
bba	Kpɑ i Gusunɔ bɛsɛn Yinni kĩɑ i n kɑ nùn mɑninɛ kpɑ i
bba	n nùn mɛm nɔɔwɑmmɛ. Domi yerɑ yɑ koo de i n wɑ̃ɑ kpɑ
bba	yu bɛɛn wɑ̃ɑru dɛnyɑsiɑ i kɑ wɑ i n wɑ̃ɑ tem mɛ
bba	sɔɔ, mɛ u bɛsɛn sikɑdobɑ Aburɑhɑmu kɑ Isɑki kɑ
bba	Mɑ Mɔwisi u womu ɡenin ɡɑri kpuro ɡeruɑ, mɑ Isirelibɑ
bba	U ben lɑɑkɑri mɔ nɡe win tiin nɔni.
bba	Bɑ win mɔru kɑ win nisinu seeyɑ
bba	Ǹ kun mɛ tɔmbu yiru bu tɔmbu nɔrɔbun subɑ wɔkuru
bba	mɑ u win tɔmbu yɑm bururɑsiɑ sɑɑ Pɑrɑnin ɡuurun di.
bba	kpɑ bu turɑre dɔ̃ɔ doke wunɛn yɑ̃ku yerɔ.
bba	Kpɑ ɑ de Isɑkɑrin bwese kɛrɑ yɑ n wɑ̃ɑ bɔri yɛndu
bba	Yerɑ Mɔwisi u kpɑm ɡeruɑ u nɛɛ,
bba	U nɛɛ, wee, nɛn sɔm kowo Mɔwisi u ɡu. Ǹ n mɛn nɑ, ɑ
bba	seewo ɑ Yuudɛni ye tɔburɑ, wunɛ kɑ Isirelibɑ kpuro i dɑ
bba	Durɔ be, bɑ nùn sɔ̃ɔwɑ bɑ nɛɛ, yèn nɔɔ mwɛɛru sɑ
bba	kuɑ kɑ bɔ̃ri mi, sɑ ko ye ko. Adɑmɑ wee ye wunɛn tii
bba	kpɑ su bu sɔ̃ mɑ Yuudɛnin dɑɑrun nim mu kokubu yɔ̃rɑ
bba	Yinni Gusunɔn kpɑkororun wuswɑɑɔ sɑnɑm mɛ bɑ kɑ tu
bba	tɔburɔ. Kpee nini nu ko n sɑ̃ɑ yen seedɑ bɛsɛ
bba	Isirelibɑn sɔ̃ sere kɑ bɑɑdommɑɔ.
bba	Durɔ wi, u wisɑ u nɛɛ, ɑɑwo, nɑ ǹ yen ɡoo. Nɑ
bba	sɑ̃ɑwɑ Yinni Gusunɔn tɑbu kowobun wiruɡii. Yen sɔ̃nɑ
bba	Mɑ bɑ kpenu ɡurɑ bɑ nin tɑkɑnu kuɑ ben wɔllɔ te tɑ
bba	wɑ̃ɑ mi sere kɑ ɡisɔ. Ye kpuron sɔ̃nɑ bɑ yɑm mi
bba	sokumɔ Akɔɔn wɔwɑ sere kɑ ɡisɔn ɡisɔ. Yĩsi ten
bba	tubusiɑnɑ, nɔni swɑ̃ɑrun wɔwɑ.
bba	U yɑ̃ku yee te bɑnɑwɑ nɡe mɛ Mɔwisi, Yinni Gusunɔn sɔm
bba	kowo u Isirelibɑ sɔ̃ɔwɑ ye u yoruɑ woodɑbɑn tireru
bba	sɔɔ. U nɛɛ, bu Yinni Gusunɔ yɑ̃ku yeru kuo kɑ kpee ni
bba	bɑ ǹ dɑ̃ke. Ye bɑ tu bɑnɑ bɑ kpɑ mɑ bɑ yɑ̃ku
bba	dɔ̃ɔ mwɑɑrɑruɡinu kɑ siɑrɑbun yɑ̃kunu kuɑ mi.
bba	Adoni Sedɛki, Yerusɑlɛmun sunɔ u nuɑ mɑ Yosue u Ayi
bba	kɑmiɑ u ye kpeerɑsiɑ u yen sunɔ ɡo, nɡe mɛ u rɑɑ
bba	Yeriko kɑ yen sunɔ kuɑ. U mɑɑ nuɑ mɑ Gɑbɑoniɡibu bɑ
bba	kɑ Isirelibɑ ɑrukɑwɑni bɔkuɑ, bɑ wɑ̃ɑ ben suunu sɔɔ.
bba	Yen biru sɑɑ Mɑkedɑn di, Yosue kɑ win tɔn be, bɑ dɑ bɑ
bba	Sinɑm be bɑ kɑmiɑ mi, ben wusu wɑ̃ɑwɑ sɑɑ ɡuu tèn mi
bba	ɡɑ̃ɑnu ku rɑ kpin berɑ ɡiɑn di Seirin bɔkuɔ, sɔ̃ɔ
bba	yɛ̃sɑn nɔm dwɑru ɡiɑ n kɑ ɡirɑri Bɑɑli Gɑdiɔ ye
bba	yɑ wɑ̃ɑ Libɑnin wɔwɑɔ ɡuu te bɑ mɔ̀ Hɛɛmɔɔn
bba	ɡɑ̃ɑrɔ sɔ̃ɔ yɛ̃sɑn nɔm ɡeu ɡiɑ.
bba	Mɛyɑ Filisitibɑn tem kɑ Gesuribɑn tem
bba	Adɑmɑ u ǹ Lefin bwese kɛrɑ tem ɡɑm wɛ̃. U bu
bba	sɔ̃ɔwɑ bu ko Gusunɔ ben Yinnin yɑ̃ku kowobu. Yeyɑ yɑ ko
bba	n sɑ̃ɑ ben tubi, nɡe mɛ Yinni Gusunɔ u ɡeruɑ.
bba	Heboronin diyɑ u seewɑ u dɑ u Debiriɡibu wɔri. Wuu ɡerɑ
bba	bɑ rɑ rɑɑ soku Sefɛɛn wuu.
bba	Kɑ mɑɑ Ekoroni, ye kɑ yen wuu mɑrosu kɑ yen bɑru kpɑɑnu.
bba	Gɑlɑdi, Mɑkirin bii, Mɑnɑsen debubu u Efɛɛ mɑrɑ. Efɛɛ
bba	wi, u Selofɑdi mɑrɑ. Selofɑdi wi, u ǹ bii tɔn durɔ
bba	mɑrɑ, sere tɔn kurɔbu tɔnɑ. Bii ben yĩsɑ wee. Mɑlɑ kɑ
bba	Nɔɑ kɑ Hoɡulɑ kɑ Milikɑ kɑ Tirisɑ.
bba	Sɔ̃ɔ yɛ̃sɑn nɔm dwɑru ɡiɑ mɑɑ, tɑ dɑwɑ sɔ̃ɔ
bba	duu yeru ɡiɑ sɑɑ Yɑrimun wuun di sere Nɛfitoɑn bwiiyɔ.
bba	Berɑ yeni kpurowɑ yɑ kuɑ Sɑbulonin bwese kɛrɑɡiɑ.
bba	Sɑnɑm mɛ Dɑnubɑ bɑ wɑ yibɛrɛbɑ bɑ kpɑm ben tem
bba	mwɛɛrimɔ, yerɑ be, bɑ mɑɑ dɑ bɑ Lesɛmu wɔri bɑ yen
bba	tɔmbu kpuro ɡo. Mɑ bɑ yɑnde sinɑ mi, yɑ kuɑ ben wuu.
bba	Yerɑ bɑ ye ben sikɑdon yĩsiru kɑ̃ te bɑ mɔ̀ Dɑnu.
bba	Wuu si kpuro, si bɑ yɑ̃ku kowo Aronin bweseru wɛ̃ su
bba	sɑ̃ɑwɑ wɔkurɑ itɑ, ɡen bɑɑɡere kɑ ɡen kpɑrɑ yenu.
bba	Mɑ Rubɛnibɑ kɑ Gɑdibɑ kɑ Mɑnɑse be, bɑ ɡɔsirɑ bɑ
bba	dɑ ben temɔ bɑ Isirelibɑn bwese kɛri yi yi tie deri,
bba	Kɑnɑnin tem mi. Bɑ dɑ bɑ sinɑ Gɑlɑdin temɔ nɡe mɛ
bba	Yinni Gusunɔ u ɡeruɑ sɑɑ win sɔm kowo Mɔwisin nɔɔn di.
bba	Yen sɔ̃, i tɛmɑnɔ, i hɑniɑ koowo kpɑ i wɑ i woodɑ ye
bba	mɛm nɔɔwɑ ye Mɔwisi u yoruɑ tireru sɔɔ kpɑ i ku yen
bba	Yosue u bu sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, bɛɛ, i bɛɛn tii seedɑ diiyɑ
bba	mɑ Yinni Gusunɔwɑ i ɡɔsɑ i sɑ̃.
bba	Yen biru Yudɑbɑ kɑ ben mɑɑbu Simɛɔbɑ bɑ Kɑnɑni be bɑ
bba	wɑ̃ɑ Sefɑtiɔ wɔri bɑ kpeerɑsiɑ mɑm mɑm. Wuu ɡerɑ
bba	bɑ yĩsiru kɑ̃ Hɔɔmɑ. Yen tubusiɑnɑ bɑnsu.
bba	12-13 Bɑ Gusunɔ ben bɑɑbɑbɑn yinni deri wi u bu yɑrɑmɑ
bba	Eɡibitin di. Mɑ bɑ be bɑ bu sikerenɛn bũu ni bɑ mɔ̀
bba	Bɑɑlibɑ kɑ Asitɑɑtebɑ sɑ̃ɑmɔ bɑ nu wiru
bba	kpĩiyɑmmɛ. Yerɑ n derɑ Yinni Gusunɔn mɔru seewɑ.
bba	Mɑ sinɑ boko u nɛɛ, win sinɑ bwɑ̃ɑbu bu ɡinɑ yɑrio be
bba	Ye bɑ Siserɑ kɑ win tɑbu kowobu kɑ win tɑbu kɛkɛbɑ
bba	wɔri, Yinni Gusunɔ u derɑ Siserɑn tɔn be, bɑ burisinɑ
bba	Bɑrɑkin wuswɑɑɔ. Mɑ Siserɑ u sɑrɑ win kɛkɛn di u
bba	Wiruɡii ɡoo sɑri wi u dɑm mɔ Isirelibɑ sɔɔ,
bba	Isɑkɑribɑn wiruɡibu bɑ kɑ Deborɑ yɔ̃rɑ.
bba	Kɑɑ domɑru wɑ, Yɑɛli, Hebɛɛ Kenin kurɔ.
bba	U bɛɛ wɔrɑ ben nɔmɑn di kɑ sere mɑɑ be bɑ bɛɛ dɑm
bba	dɔremɔ kpuron nɔmɑn di. Mɑ u be kpuro ɡirɑ bɛɛn
bba	wuswɑɑn di. U ben tem mwɑ u bɛɛ wɛ̃.
bba	Wee, kon yɑ̃ɑ sɑn sini yi temɔ ɑlikɑmɑ soo yerɔ. Ǹ n
bba	kuɑ bururu, dirum mù n wɑ̃ɑ yɑ̃ɑ sɑn si tɔnɑ sɔɔ,
bba	kpɑ ɑlikɑmɑ soo yee te kpuro tɑ n ɡbere, sɑnɑm mɛ
bba	sɔɔrɑ kon ɡiɑ mɑ ɡeemɑ, kɑɑ Isirelibɑ fɑɑbɑ kowɑ
bba	sɑɑ nɛn min di nɡe mɛ ɑ ɡeruɑ.
bba	Yerɑ Efɑrɑimubɑ kpuro bɑ mɛnnɑ bɑ dɑ bɑ swɑɑ burɑ
bba	Yuudɛnin tɔbusun di sere n kɑ ɡirɑri Bɛti Bɑrɑɔ.
bba	N deemɑ Mɑdiɑnibɑ bɑ swɑɑ tonku wurɑɡinu mɔ, domi bɑ
bba	sɑ̃ɑwɑ Isimɛɛlin bweseru.
bba	Tɛ̃ ye i Gedeoni kɑ win yɛnuɡibu kuɑ mi, ì n ye kuɑn nɑ
bba	kɑ nuku tiɑ murɑfitiru sɑri, Gusunɔ u de bɛɛ kɑ
bba	Abimɛlɛki i n wɑ̃ɑsinɛ kɑ nuku dobu.
bba	Mɑ ben bɑɑwure u dɑ̃ɑ kɑ̃ɑsɑ burɑ u seru sɔndi bɑ
bba	kɑ nùn swĩi. Mɑ be kpuro bɑ ben dɑ̃ɑ ye sure wɔru ɡen
bba	kɔnnɔwɔ. Yen biru bɑ ye dɔ̃ɔ doke. Mɑ Sikɛmuɡii be bɑ
bba	wɑ̃ɑ wɔru ɡe sɔɔ kpuro bɑ dɔ̃ɔ mwɑɑrɑ. Bɑ
bba	sɑ̃ɑwɑ tɔmbu nɔrɔbu (1.000), kurɔbu kɑ durɔbu.
bba	Yen biru Amɔnibɑ bɑ Isirelibɑ wɔri.
bba	Sɑnɑm mɛ u bii wi wɑ, yerɑ u win tiin yɑberu nɛnuɑ u
bba	kɑrɑnɑ nuku sɑnkirɑnun sɔ̃, u nɔɔɡiru suɑ u nɛɛ,
bba	nɛn bii, nuku sɑnkirɑ bɑkɑnu sɔɔrɑ ɑ mɑn doke mi. Domi
bba	nɑ Yinni Gusunɔ nɔɔ mwɛɛru kuɑ. Tɑǹ mɑɑ kɔbiɑrɔ.
bba	Mɑ Gusunɔ u Mɑnɔɑn kɑnɑru mwɑ, u derɑ win ɡɔrɑdo wi,
bba	u wurɑ kurɔ win mi, mi u sɔ̃ ɡberɔ. Adɑmɑ win durɔ
bba	Mɑ Sɑnsom u bu sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, kon bɛɛ sukuru ɡɑru
bba	kuɑ. Sere n kɑ ko kurɔ kpɑɑ ten sɔ̃ɔ nɔɔbɑ yiru, kpɑ
bba	i mɑn tu tubusiɑ. Ì n tu tubɑ, kon bɛɛn bɑɑwure yɑberu
bba	Sɑnsom u bu wisɑ u nɛɛ, nɡe mɛ ben tii bɑ mɑn kuɑ, nɡe
bba	Ye Sɑnsom u dweeyɑ, mɑ Dɑlilɑ u win wirun tɑri yi mɛnnɑ
bba	kɑ wɛ̃ɛ siiri u wesɑ. Mɑ u kɑ yi dɑ̃ru kpɑresi temɔ.
bba	Yerɑ u nùn yɑmiɑ u nɛɛ, Sɑnsom, Filisitibɑ wee, bɑ nun
bba	N deemɑ Mikɑ u rɑɑ sɑ̃ɑ yeru mɔ win yɛnuɔ. Mɑ u derɑ
bba	bɑ nùn bwɑ̃ɑroku ɡɑnu kuɑ. Mɑ u win tiin bii turo
bba	ɡɔsɑ u kuɑ nin yɑ̃ku kowo.
bba	Mɑ Dɑnu be, bɑ ɡurenɑ bɑ doonɑ, bɑ ben bibu ɡbiisie kɑ
bba	yɑɑ sɑbenu kɑ sere ben sɔmunu.
bba	Mɑ u kɑ tɔn be dɑ win yɛnuɔ u ben kɛtɛkunu dĩɑnu
bba	wɛ̃. Ben tii bɑ ben nɑɑsu kpɑkiɑ, mɑ u bu dĩɑnu wɛ̃
bba	Mɑ Isireli be, bɑ dɑ Betɛliɔ bu kɑ Gusunɔ bikiɑ u bu
bba	sɔ̃ɔsi bwese kɛrɑ ye yɑ koo ɡbi yu Bɛnyɑmɛɛbɑ wɔri.
bba	Mɑ Yinni Gusunɔ u Yudɑbɑ ɡɔsɑ.
bba	Isirelibɑ bɑ ɡɔsirɑmɑ bɑ nɑ Bɛnyɑmɛɛ be bɑ tien
bba	wusu sɔɔ. Bɑ bu ɡo ɡo sere kɑ ben yɑɑ sɑbenɔ. Hunde
bba	koni ye yɑ wɑ̃ɑ mi kpuro ɡesi, bɑ ɡowɑ. Mɑ bɑ ben wuu
bba	6-7 Yenibɑn biru, Nɑomi u nuɑ Gusunɔ u win tɔmbu durom kuɑ
bba	u bu dĩɑnu wɛ̃. Yerɑ u seewɑ sɔ̃ɔ teeru kɑ win biɡii
bba	kurɔbu Mɔɑbun di, bɑ wiɔ Yudɑn temɔ.
bba	Sɑnɑm mɛ bɑ dimɔ, Boɑsi u nùn sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, ɑ
bba	susimɑ ɑ pɛ̃ɛ suɑ ɑ sɔ̃re kpee sɔɔ kpɑ ɑ di.
bba	Yen biru, u dwɑɑ mɛro sɑɑriɑ ye Boɑsi u nùn kuɑ.
bba	Adɑmɑ Hɑnɑɡiɑ u rɑ de yɑ n kpɑ̃ɑru bo. Domi u nùn
bba	kĩ bɑɑ mɛ Yinni Gusunɔ u nùn kuɑ wĩro.
bba	U sɑ̃ɑwɑ nɡe kpee bɑɑ mi nɑ rɑ kuke.
bba	Adɑmɑ u koo de tɔn kɔ̃sobu
bba	Yen sɔ̃, u nɛɛ, wiyɑ u rɑɑ ɡeruɑ mɑ wunɛn yɛnu kɑ
bba	wunɛn bɑɑbɑn yɛnuɡibu bɑ koo ko win yɑ̃ku kowobu sere
bba	kɑ bɑɑdommɑɔ. Adɑmɑ tɛ̃ u ɡeruɑ u nɛɛ, yɑ ǹ
bba	mɑɑ koorɔ mɛ, domi be bɑ nùn bɛɛrɛ wɛ̃ɛmɔ, beyɑ u
bba	koo bɛɛrɛ wɛ̃. Be bɑ kun nùn ɡɑrɑ, beyɑ u ǹ
bba	Sɑmuɛli u kpunɑ sere n kɑ kuɑ sisiru. Mɑ u sɑ̃ɑ yerun
bba	ɡɑmbobɑ kɛniɑ. Adɑmɑ u ǹ kɑ̃kɑ u Eli kɑ̃si ten
bba	Filisitibɑ bɑ Gusunɔn woodɑn kpɑkoro te suɑ sɑɑ Ebɛni
bba	Esɛɛn di bɑ kɑ dɑ Asidɔduɔ,
bba	Bwisinun weenɑsii ni Filisitibɑ bɑ kuɑ kɑ wurɑ bɑ Yinni
bba	Gusunɔ wɛ̃ ben durum sɔ̃, bɑ nu kuɑwɑ wuu sinin sɔ̃,
bba	Asidɔdu kɑ Gɑsɑ kɑ Asikɑloni kɑ Gɑti kɑ mɑɑ Ekoroni.
bba	Mɑ Sɑmuɛli u Yinni Gusunɔn ɡɑri yi kpuro tɔn be tusiɑ.
bba	Sɑmuɛli u Sɔɔlu wisɑ u nɛɛ, nɛnɑ yɑm wɑo wi. A nɑ su
bba	dɑ ɡunɡuru mi. Sɑnnɑ sɑ ko di ɡisɔ. Ǹ n kuɑ bururu,
bba	ye ɑ bwisikumɔ wunɛn ɡɔ̃ruɔ ɑ bikiɑ, kon nun ye kpuro
bba	Adɑmɑ wee, i nùn yinɑ ɡisɔ, wi u bɛɛ fɑɑbɑ kuɑ
bba	bɛɛn wɑhɑlɑ kɑ bɛɛn nɔni swɑ̃ɑrun di. Mɑ i nɛɛ, u
bba	bɛɛ sunɔ kuo, u bɛɛ kpɑrɑ. Ǹ n mɛn nɑ, i yɑrimɑ
bba	bweseru kɑ bweseru, kpɑ i tii tusiɑ yɛnu kɑ yɛnu win
bba	Bɑ nɛɛ, ɑ ǹ sun tɑki diire, ɑ ǹ mɑɑ sun dɑm
bba	dɔrere. Mɛyɑ ɑ ǹ mɑɑ bɛsɛn ɡoon kɛ̃ru mwɑɑre ɑ
bba	Bɑ tɛ mi, bɑ kuɑwɑ sɔ̃ɔ nɔɔbɑ yiru nɡe mɛ Sɑmuɛli
bba	u Sɔɔlu burɑ, ɑdɑmɑ Sɑmuɛli u ǹ nɛ. Yerɑ tɔmbɑ
bba	Ben tɑbun tore ye sɔɔ, be yiru ye, bɑ tɔmbu ɡowɑ nɡe
bba	tɔnu yɛndun sɑkɑ bɑtumɑ piibu sɔɔ.
bba	Yerɑ Sɔɔlu u nɛɛ, i mɛnnɑmɑ bɛɛ be i sɑ̃ɑ wiruɡibu
bba	kpɑ su ɡiɑ mi torɑrɑ wɑ̃ɑ ɡisɔ.
bba	Ye Sɑmuɛli u ɡɑri yi nuɑ, yerɑ u mɔru kuɑ ɡem ɡem, mɑ
bba	u Yinni Gusunɔ nɔɔɡiru sue wɔ̃ku ɡiriru.
bba	Mɑ Yinni Gusunɔ u nɛɛ, ɑ nɑɑ ɡbiibɑ suo kpɑ ɑ nɛɛ,
bba	ɑ nɑwɑ ɑ kɑ mɑn yɑ̃kuru kuɑ.
bba	U mɑɑ sii ɡɑndun kɔrɔm doke, mɑ u sii ɡɑndun yɑɑsɑ
bba	Yinni Gusunɔ wi u mɑn wɔrɑ sɑɑ ɡbee sunɔ kɑ yɑɑ
bba	kɔ̃sɑ yen min di u koo mɑɑ mɑn wɔrɑ Filisiti win nɔmɑn
bba	Sɑɑ yè sɔɔ tɑbu kowobɑ wee tɑbu ɡberun di, mi Dɑfidi u
bba	Filisiti wi ɡo, yerɑ tɔn kurɔbɑ yɑrimɑ Isirelibɑn wusu
bba	kpuron di bu kɑ Sɔɔlu sennɑ. Bɑ yɑɑmɔ bɑ bɑrɑnu kɑ
bba	mɔrɔkunu soomɔ, bɑ kuuki mɔ̀ kɑ nuku dobu.
bba	Ye bɑ nɑ mi, Yonɑtɑm u win bɑɑ Dɑfidin ɡeɑ sɑɑriɑ u
bba	nɛɛ, wunɛ sunɔ ɑ ku wunɛn bɔ̃ɔ Dɑfidi torɑri. U ǹ
bba	nun kɔ̃sɑ ɡɑɑ kue. Ye u kuɑ kpuro, ɡɑ̃ɑ ɡeenɑ.
bba	Yonɑtɑm u nɛɛ, ɑ ku yenin bweseru bwisiku. Nɑ̀ n ɡiɑ
bba	mɑ nɛn tundo u kĩ u nun kɔ̃sɑ kuɑ, kon nun sɔ̃.
bba	Sɑɑ ye bii wi, u turɑ deedeeru mi sɛ̃u ɡe, ɡɑ dɑ, yerɑ
bba	Yonɑtɑm u kpɑm ɡbɑ̃rɑ u nɛɛ, ɡɑ wɑ̃ɑ wunɛn
bba	Mɑ Dɑfidi u seewɑ u dɑ u wɑ̃ɑ dɑ̃ɑ sɔ̃ɔ ɡe bɑ
bba	Yerɑ Sɔɔlu u win tɑbu kowobu kpuro mɛnnɑ bu dɑ bu kɑ
bba	Keilɑ wɔri, kpɑ bu Dɑfidi kɑ win tɔmbu tɑrusi.
bba	Mɑ Sɔɔlu u seewɑ u yɑrɑ u doonɑ min di.
bba	Yerɑ Nɑbɑlin sɔm kowo turo u nɑ u Abiɡɑli sɔ̃ɔwɑ u
bba	nɛɛ, wee, Dɑfidi u bɛsɛn yinni sɔmɔbu ɡɔriɑmɑ sɑɑ
bba	ɡbɑburun di bu nùn tɔbiri. Adɑmɑ u bu ɡirɑ kɑ dɑm,
bba	Dɑfidi u rɑɑ mɑɑ Akinɔɑmu Yisirɛɛliɡii suɑ kurɔ. Mɑ
bba	be yiru ye, bɑ mɔre win mi.
bba	Yenibɑn biru, Dɑfidi u tii sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, sɔ̃ɔ teeru
bba	Sɔɔlu u koo mɑn nɔmɑ turi u ɡo. Yen sɔ̃, n burɑm bo n
bba	dukɑ yɑkurɑ minin di n kpikiru dɑ Filisitibɑn temɔ kpɑ
bba	Sɔɔlu u ku mɑɑ mɑn kɑsu Isirelibɑn tem kpuro sɔɔ. Nɡe
bba	mɛyɑ kon kɑ wɑ n kisirɑ win nɔmɑn di.

bba	tem ɡirɑri u nùn bɛɛrɛ wɛ̃.
bba	Mɑ Dɑfidin nuki sɑnkirɑ too domi win tɔmbu bɑ ɡerunɑmɔ
bba	bɑ mɔ̀ bu nùn kpenu kɑsuku bu ɡo, yèn sɔ̃ bɑ ben
bba	kurɔbu kɑ bibu biɑ. Yerɑ n derɑ bɑ nuki sɑnkire. Adɑmɑ
bba	Dɑfidi u tii deri Yinni Gusunɔn nɔmuɔ. Mɑ u nùn dɑm kɑ̃.
bba	kɑ Heboroniɡibu kɑ sere mɑɑ bèn mi wi Dɑfidi kɑ win
bba	14-16 Dɑfidi kpɑm nùn bikiɑ u nɛɛ, ɑmɔnɑ ɑ kɑ
bba	kɑ̃kɑ ɑ wi Yinni Gusunɔ ɡɔsɑ nɔmɑ doke ɑ ɡo. Yen

bba	tiin nɔɔwɑ ɡɑ seedɑ di mɑ ɑ wi Yinni Gusunɔ ɡɔsɑ ɡo.
bba	Dɑmɡibɑ wɔrukɑ tɑbu ɡberɔ.
bba	Yerɑ u dɔmɑ te Abinɛɛ nɑɑ ɡirɑ, u ǹ wure u nùn deri
bba	Mɑ Pɑtiɛli wi, u Mikɑli swĩi u sumɔ sere bɑ kɑ turɑ
bba	Bɑhurimuɔ. Mɑ Abinɛɛ u nùn sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, ɑ den
bba	ɡɔsiro. Yerɑ u ɡɔsirɑ u wurɑ win yɛnuɔ.

bba	bɑ mɔ̀ Mɛfibosɛti. Bii wi, u kuɑ yɛmɔ. Wɔ̃ɔ
bba	nɔɔbuwɑ u mɔ sɑnɑm mɛ Sɔɔlu kɑ Yonɑtɑm bɑ ɡu
bba	Yisirɛɛliɔ tɑbu sɔɔ. Ye kurɔ wi u bii wi nɔɔrimɔ u
bba	ɡɔɔ win lɑbɑɑri nuɑ, yerɑ u bii wi suɑ u kɑ doonɔ. Ye

bba	ɡɑmbo dokemɔ mɑ win bii dɑ̃ɑko Seɡubu u mɑɑ ɡu. N
bba	deemɑ Yinni Gusunɔ u rɑɑ ɡeruɑ Yosue Nunin biin nɔɔn di
bba	u nɛɛ, wi u mɑɑ wuu ɡe bɑnɑ, mɛsumɑ yɛ̃ron bibu bɑ
bba	Mɑ Akɑbu kɑ Abudiɑsi, bɑ yɑm mi bɔnu kuɑ, bɑ yɑkɑ
bba	bekusu kɑso wɔri. Ben bɑɑwure u win swɑɑ mwɑ.
bba	Mɑ bɑ kuɑ mɛ. Mɑ u mɑɑ nɛɛ, bu wureo bu nim mɛ wisi.
bba	Mɑ dɔ̃ɔ u mɑɑ nɑ. Mɛyɑ Yinni Gusunɔ kun wɑ̃ɑ
bba	dɔ̃ɔ wi sɔɔ. Yen biru dɑmu piibu ɡɑɡɑ mɑɑ nɑ ɡe
bba	Isirelibɑn berɑ kɑ berɑn tɑbu kowo be, bɑ ɡbiɑ bɑ tɑbu
bba	yɑrɑ. Yerɑ Bɛni Hɑdɑdi u bikiɑ u nɛɛ, berɑ̀ mini. Mɑ
bba	bɑ nùn wisɑ bɑ nɛɛ, Sɑmɑrin diyɑ bɑ yɑrimɑ.
bba	Sɑnɑm mɛ sinɑ boko u sɑrɔ win bɔkuɔ, yerɑ u nɔɔɡiru
bba	suɑ u nɛɛ, wee nɑ rɑɑ wɑ̃ɑ tɑbu sĩɑ sɔɔ, mɑ
bba	subɑru sɔɔ ɡoo u yɑrɑ u kɑ mɑn tɑbu durɔ ɡoo nɑɑwɑ
bba	n nùn kɔ̃su. U nɛɛ, nɑ̀ n derɑ durɔ wi, u doonɑ,
bba	nɛnɑ kon ko win kɔsire, ǹ kun mɛ, kon sii ɡeesun ɡobi
bba	nɔrɔbun subɑ itɑ (3.000) kɔsiɑ.
bba	Domi ɡoo sɑri wi u tii yɔ̃su kɔ̃sɑ sɔɔ nɡe Akɑbu,
bba	Yinni Gusunɔn wuswɑɑɔ. N deemɑ win kurɔ Yesɑbɛliwɑ u
bba	rɑ n nùn dɑm kɛ̃mɔ u kɑ ye ko.
bba	Yerɑ Misee u Akɑbu sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, ɑ Yinni Gusunɔn
bba	ɡɑri swɑɑ dɑkio, nɑ nùn wɑ u sɔ̃ win sinɑ kitɑru
bba	wɔllɔ. Mɑ win tɑbu kowobu bɑ yɔ̃ win nɔm ɡeu kɑ win
bba	Yosɑfɑti u ɡoo nimkusu dɑ̃kɑ si bɑ ko n dɑ kɑ wurɑ
bba	kɑso de Ofiriɔ. Adɑmɑ su ku rɑ turi mi, su rɑ kɔsirewɑ
bba	swɑɑɔ, wuu ɡe bɑ mɔ̀ Ɛsioni Gebɛɛɔ.
bba	Mɑ Elisee u nùn wisɑ u nɛɛ, sere kɑ Yinni Gusunɔn
bba	wɑ̃ɑru kɑ mɑɑ wunɛn tiiɡiru nɑ ǹ nun derimɔ.
bba	Yerɑ u bu sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, bu ɡbɛ̃ɛ kpɑɑru tɑmɑ bu
bba	Yen sisiru bururu, sɑɑ ye bɑ kĩ bu bururun yɑ̃kuru ko,
bba	yerɑ bɑ wɑ wee, nim mu wee, sɑɑ Edɔmun berɑ ɡiɑn di, mu
bba	Yen biruwɑ kurɔ wi, u ɡurɑ suɑ u bii tɔn durɔ mɑrɑ
bba	wɔ̃ɔ kpɔɔ ɡe sɔɔ, ɡe Elisee u nùn burɑ.
bba	Yenibɑn biru, durɔ ɡoo u nɑ sɑɑ Bɑɑli Sɑlisɑn di u kɑ
bba	Elisee pɛ̃ɛ nɑɑwɑ, ye bɑ kuɑ kɑ ɔɔsun som kpɑm kɑ
bba	sere mɑɑ dĩɑ bimi kpɛɛ ɡɛɛn sɑɑki tiɑ. Yerɑ Elisee
bba	u win sɔm kowo sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, u ye bɔnu koowo tɔn be bɑ
bba	Nɑmɑni u nùn kɔkurɑ u nɛɛ, ɑ yɑnde kilo wɑtɑ suo.
bba	Mɑ Siriɡii be, bɑ dɑ Eliseen mi. Yerɑ Elisee u kɑnɑru
bba	kuɑ u nɛɛ, Yinni Gusunɔ, ɑ bu wɔ̃koru kpɛ̃ɛyɔ.
bba	Yerɑ sinɑ boko u seewɑ wɔ̃kuru u win bwɑ̃ɑbu sɔ̃ɔwɑ
bba	u nɛɛ, kon bɛɛ sɔ̃ bwisi yi Siriɡibu bɑ sun kuɑ. Bɑ
bba	yɛ̃ mɑ sɑ wɑ̃ɑ ɡɔ̃ɔru sɔɔ, yen sɔ̃nɑ bɑ ben
bba	sɑnsɑni deri bɑ dɑ bɑ kukuɑ yɑkɑsɔ, mɑ bɑ nɛɛ,
bba	bɛsɛ Isirelibɑ sɑ̀ n yɑrɑ bɛsɛn wuun di, kpɑ bu sun
bba	mwɛɛri wɑsiru. Yen biru bu du bɛsɛn wuuɔ.
bba	Adɑmɑ Yinni Gusunɔ u ǹ kĩ u Yudɑbɑn bweseru kpeerɑsiɑ
bba	win bɔ̃ɔ Dɑfidin sɔ̃. Domi u rɑɑ nùn nɔɔ mwɛɛru
bba	kuɑ mɑ win bibun bweserɑ tɑ ko n wɑ̃ɑ bɑn te sɔɔ sere
bba	N deemɑ Yorɑmu wi, u ɡinɑ wɑ̃ɑ Yisirɛɛliɔ bɑ nùn
bba	nɔɔrimɔ mɛɛrɑ ye u wɑn sɔ̃ sɑnɑm mɛ u tɑbu mɔ̀
bba	bɛɛ be i sinɑ bokon bibu kɔ̃su kɑ win tɑbu kɛkɛ yi dumi
bba	ɡɑwe, kɑ win dumi kɑ wuu ɡbɑ̃rɑruɡuu kɑ win tɑbu
bba	yɑ̃nu, tire teni tɑ̀ n bɛɛn nɔmɑ duɑ, ye ko i ko wee,
bba	Mɑ bɑ duɑ mi, bɑ bu ɡo ɡo kɑ tɑkobi. Yerɑ bɑ ɡoo ni
bba	yɑrɑ bɑ kɑ dɑ wuun biruɔ. Yen biru bɑ ɡɔsirɑ bɑ wurɑ
bba	1-2 Yehun bɑndun wɔ̃ɔ nɔɔbɑ yiruse sɔɔrɑ Yoɑsi u
bba	bɑndu di Yerusɑlɛmuɔ. U mɔwɑ wɔ̃ɔ nɔɔbɑ yiru sɑɑ
bba	ye sɔɔ. Mɑ u kuɑ wɔ̃ɔ weeru bɑn te sɔɔ. Win mɛron
bba	yĩsirɑ Sibiɑ Beri Sebɑɡii.
bba	Ye Yoɑsi u kuɑn sukum kɑ wɔruɡɔɔ te u sɔ̃ɔsi, kɑ sere
bba	mɑɑ tɑɑ bi u kuɑ kɑ Amɑsiɑ Yudɑbɑn sinɑ boko, ye
bba	kpuron ɡɑri yi yoruɑ Isirelibɑn sinɑmbun fɑɑɡin tireru
bba	Mɑ u dɑ u wurɑ ɡurɑ, kɑ sii ɡeesu kɑ sere ɡɑ̃ɑ ɡee
bba	ni nu wɑ̃ɑ Yinni Gusunɔn sɑ̃ɑ yerɔ kɑ sinɑmbun
bba	ɑrumɑnin beru yerɔ. Yen biru u mɑɑ tɔmbu mɔɔru
bba	mwɛɛrɑ. Mɑ u ɡɔsirɑ Sɑmɑriɔ.
bba	Yen biruwɑ Mɛnɑhɛmu wi, u wuu ɡe bɑ mɔ̀ Tifusɑki wɔri.
bba	Mɑ u tɔmbu ɡo sɑɑ Tirisɑn di n kɑ dɑ Tifusɑki mi. U
bba	Tifusɑki ye wɔriwɑ kɑ dɑm yèn sɔ̃ tɔn be, bɑ yinɑ u
bba	du ben wuuɔ, mɑ u ben ɡuriɡibun nuki bɛsukɑ.
bba	Mɑ Akɑsi u sii ɡeesu suɑ kɑ wurɑ ye yɑ wɑ̃ɑ Yinni
bba	Gusunɔn sɑ̃ɑ yerɔ, kɑ sinɑmbun ɑrumɑni beru yerɔ. Mɑ
bba	u ye kpuro ɡurɑ u Asirin sinɑ boko wɛ̃.
bba	Yudɑbɑn tii, bɑ ǹ Gusunɔ ben Yinni mɛm nɔɔwɛ.
bba	Isirelibɑn yirɑ bɑ swĩi mɑm mɑm.
bba	Esekiɑsi Yudɑbɑn sinɑ boko win bɑndun wɔ̃ɔ nnɛse sɔɔ,
bba	kɑ mɑɑ Osee, Elɑn bii, Isirelibɑn sinɑ bokon bɑndun
bba	wɔ̃ɔ nɔɔbɑ yiruse sɔɔ, yerɑ Sɑɑmɑnɑsɑɑ Asirin
bba	sinɑ boko kɑ win tɔmbu bɑ Sɑmɑri tɑrusi wɔ̃ɔ yiru.
bba	Yerɑ u Eliɑkimu sɔm kowobun wiruɡii kɑ mɑɑ Sebinɑ win
bba	tire yoro kɑ yɑ̃ku kowo ɡuro ɡurobu ɡɔrɑ Gusunɔn sɔmɔ
bba	Esɑi Amɔtin biin mi. N deemɑ be mɑɑ, sɑɑkibɑrɑ bɑ
bba	u ɡen dɑ̃ɑ ɡeɑ ye bɑ mɔ̀ sɛduru kɑ sipɛrɛ
bba	Ye n kuɑ wɔ̃kuru yerɑ Yinni Gusunɔn ɡɔrɑdo u yɑrɑ u
bba	dɑ Asiriɡibun sɑnsɑniɔ mɑ u tɔnu nɔrɔbun subɑ wunɑɑ
bba	wɛnɛ kɑ nɔɔbu (185.000) ɡo. Ye bɑ seewɑ bururu, bɑ
bba	Mɑ u turɑnu kuɑ mi bɑ rɑ sɔ̃ɔ kɑ suru kɑ kperi sɑ̃
bba	sɑ̃ɑ yerun yɑɑri yiru sɔɔ.
bba	Mɑ u mɑɑ nɛɛ, tireru ɡɑru wee te yɑ̃ku kowo tɔnwero
bba	Mɑ sinɑ boko u nɛɛ, i tu derio ɡoo u ku rɑɑ win kukunu
bba	Sɑɑ ye sɔɔrɑ Bɑbilonin sinɑ boko Nɛbukɑnɛsɑɑn tɑbu
bba	kowobu bɑ nɑ bɑ Yerusɑlɛmu wɔri bɑ ye tɑrusi.
bba	Be kpurowɑ u suɑ u kɑ Bɑbilonin sinɑ boko dɑɑwɑ
bba	Yokutɑniwɑ u Alimɔdɑdi mɑrɑ, kɑ Selɛfu, kɑ
bba	Ye Bɑɑli Hɑnɑni u ɡu, mɑ Hɑdɑri, Pɑiɡii, u ɡɔnɑ
bba	kɔsire kuɑ. Win kurɔn yĩsirɑ Mɛhetɑbɛli, Mɑtiredin bii,
bba	Rɑmu, Yerɑmɛɛlin bii ɡbiikoon bibɑ Mɑɑsi, kɑ Yɑmini,
bba	Mɑ Sefɑtiɑ, Abitɑlin bii u sɑ̃ɑ nɔɔbuse. Mɑ
bba	Yitireɑmu, Eɡilɑn bii u sɑ̃ɑ nɔɔbɑ tiɑse. Eɡilɑ wi,
bba	u mɑɑ sɑ̃ɑwɑ Dɑfidin kurɔbun turo.
bba	Mɑ Gusunɔ u nùn kuɑ ye u bikiɑ.
bba	Isirelin bii be sɔɔ, Yudɑwɑ u dɑm bo. Win bwese kɛrɑn
bba	diyɑ kpɑro u yɑrɑ. Adɑmɑ Yosɛfun bibɑ bɑ yerumɑru
bba	Ye Usi u seewɑ, mɑ u Serɑyɑ mɑrɑ. Mɑ Serɑyɑ u seewɑ u
bba	kɑ mɑɑ Ɛlikɑnɑ ɡoo, kɑ Yoɛli ɡoo kɑ Asɑriɑ, kɑ
bba	Wuu si bɑ bu wɛ̃, siyɑ Sikɛmu ye yɑ wɑ̃ɑ Efɑrɑimun
bba	ɡuurɔ, kɑ yen kpɑrɑ yenu. Miyɑ bɑ ko n dɑ kpikiru de.
bba	Kɑ Gesɛɛ kɑ yen kpɑrɑ yenu,
bba	Beniwɑ bɑ sɑ̃ɑ Gɑlɑdi, Mɑkirin bii, Mɑnɑsen debubun
bba	berɑ Nɑmɑni kɑ Akiyɑ kɑ sere Gerɑ. Gerɑ wi u kɑ bu dɑ
bba	mi, wiyɑ u Usɑ kɑ Ahihudu mɑrɑ.
bba	Siloniɡibun bwese kɛrɑ sɔɔrɑ Asɑyɑ u wɑ̃ɑ kɑ win
bba	bibu. Asɑyɑ wiyɑ u sɑ̃ɑ win bii ɡbiikoo.
bba	Win bii ɡbiikoowɑ Abudoni. Be bɑ mɑɑ tie, berɑ Suri kɑ
bba	Kisi kɑ Bɑɑli kɑ Nɛri kɑ Nɑdɑbu,
bba	Dɑfidi u dɑ u sinɑ wuu ɡbɑ̃rɑruɡuu ɡen mi. Yen sɔ̃nɑ
bba	kɑ Hefɛɛ, Mɛkerɑɡii, kɑ Akiyɑ, Pɑloniɡii,
bba	Domi Gusunɔ wunɛn Yinni u nun fɑɑbɑ kuɑ.
bba	Mɑ Dɑfidi kɑ Isirelibɑ kpuro bɑ bu swĩi bɑ mɔrɔkunu
bba	soomɔ kɑ ɡɔ̃ɔɡenu, kɑ bɑrɑ kpɑ̃nu, kɑ
bba	sɛkɛtirɛnu, kɑ yɑnkokonu. Mɑ bɑ womusu mɔ̀ bɑ yɑɑmɔ
bba	kɑ ben dɑm kpuro bɑ kɑ Gusunɔ sɑ̃ɑmɔ.
bba	Mɛrɑrin bwese kɛrɑ sɔɔ, Asɑyɑwɑ u sɑ̃ɑ wiruɡii, kɑ
bba	wiɡibu tɔmbu ɡoobu kɑ yɛndu (220).
bba	i Yinni Gusunɔ siɑro, kpɑ i nùn sɑ̃,
bba	I ku mɑɑ nɛn sɔmɔbu kɔ̃sɑ kuɑ.
bba	Dɑ̃nu, i nuku dobun kuuki koowo
bba	nɡe mɛ bɑ bu kuɑ yellu kpɑrobun wɑɑti sɔɔ. Nɑ win
bba	yibɛrɛbɑ kpuro sekuru doke. Nɛ, Yinni Gusunɔwɑ nɑ nùn
bba	sɔ̃ɔmɔ mɑ kon nùn ko bwese bɑkɑrun nuuru.
bba	Dɑfidi u bɑndu di Isirelibɑ kpuro sɔɔ. Mɑ u ɡeɑ mɔ̀, u
bba	Sɔ̃ɔ teeru Setɑm u Isirelibɑ seesi, mɑ u Dɑfidi bɔrie u
bba	Mɑ Dɑfidi u nɛɛ, yɑm miniwɑ bɑ koo Yinni Gusunɔn sɑ̃ɑ
bba	yeru bɑni. Miyɑ yɑ̃ku yerɑ ko n mɑɑ wɑ̃ɑ mi Isirelibɑ
bba	bɑ ko n dɑ yɑ̃ku dɔ̃ɔ mwɑɑrɑruɡinu ko.
bba	Amurɑmun bibɑ Aroni kɑ Mɔwisi. Mɑ bɑ Aroni kɑ win bibun
bba	bweseru ɡɔsɑ bɑ yi nɛnɛm sere kɑ bɑɑdommɑɔ bɑ n dɑ
bba	kɑ Yinni Gusunɔ turɑre dɔ̃ɔ dokeye, kpɑ bɑ n dɑ mɑɑ
bba	sɑ̃ɑrun sɔmburu ko, kpɑ bɑ n dɑ mɑɑ tɔmbu domɑru kue
bba	Mɑ Mɑɑkiyɑ u sɑ̃ɑ nɔɔbuse.
bba	Musin bibun bweseru sɔɔ, Mɑkili kɑ Edɛɛ kɑ Yerimɔtiwɑ.
bba	Mɑ Eliɑtɑ u sɑ̃ɑ yɛnduse.
bba	N deemɑ ɑrumɑni ye bɑ tɑbu di, yen sukumɑ bɑ kɑ Yinni
bba	Gusunɔ nɑɑwɑ bu kɑ win sɑ̃ɑ yeru sɔmɛ.
bba	Mɑnɑsen bwese kɛrɑn sukumɡibu sɔɔ, be bɑ mɑɑ wɑ̃ɑ
bba	sɔ̃ɔ yɑri yeru ɡiɑ, Gɑlɑdin temɔ, Ido, Sɑkɑrin biiwɑ
bba	Tɛ̃, ɑ n yɛ̃ mɑ Yinni Gusunɔ u nun ɡɔsɑwɑ ɑ kɑ nùn
bba	diru bɑniɑ mi bɑ ko n dɑ nùn sɑ̃. Yen sɔ̃ ɑ de ɑ n
bba	wɔruɡɔru mɔ kpɑ ɑ se ɑ sɔmburu ko.
bba	Dɑfidi u mɑɑ tɔn be bɑ mɛnnɛ mi kpuro sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ,
bba	i Gusunɔ bɛɛn Yinni siɑro.
bba	Yerɑ u tɔmbu nɔrɔbun subɑ wɑtɑ kɑ wɔkuru (70.000)
bba	ɡɔsɑ be bɑ ko n dɑ sɔmunu sue, kɑ tɔmbu nɔrɔbun subɑ
bba	wɛnɛ (80.000) be bɑ ko n dɑ kpenu dɑ̃ku ɡuunɔ. Mɑ u
bba	mɑɑ tɔmbu nɔrɔbun subɑ itɑ kɑ nɑtɑ (3.600) ɡɔsɑ be
bba	bɑ ko n sɔmbu te nɔni doke.
bba	U dii ten wuswɑɑɔ ɡbere yiru kuɑ. Yen bɑɑyeren ɡunum mu
bba	sɑ̃ɑwɑ ɡɔm soonu tɛnɑ kɑ nɔɔbu. Mɑ bɑ ye furɔsu
bba	sɔndiɑ wɔllɔ. Sin ɡunum mu sɑ̃ɑwɑ ɡɔm soonu nɔɔbu.
bba	U mɑɑ dii te tɑ dɛɛre ɡem ɡem ɡɑmbobɑ kɑ sɑ̃ɑ yee
bba	ten tiin kɔnnɔn ɡɑmbobɑ kuɑ kɑ wurɑ.
bba	Gusunɔ, bɛsɛ Isirelibɑn Yinni, ɡoo mɑɑ sɑri nɡe wunɛ
bba	wɔllɔ kɑ temɔ. Wunɛn bwɑ̃ɑ be bɑ nun mɛm nɔɔwɑmmɛ
bba	kɑ ɡɔ̃ru tiɑ, ɑ rɑ ɑrukɑwɑni ye ɑ kɑ bu bɔkuɑ
bba	yibie, kpɑ ɑ bu wunɛn wɔnwɔndu sɔ̃ɔsi.
bba	Kpɑ be bɑ nun mɛm nɔɔwɑmmɛ
bba	U Bɛti Horoni ye yɑ wɑ̃ɑ ɡunɡuru wɔllɔ kɑ ye yɑ
bba	wɑ̃ɑ wɔwɑɔ bɑnɑ. Wuu si, su ɡbɑ̃rɑnu kɑ ɡɑmbobɑ
bba	mɔ, kɑ mɑɑ yen sɛ̃retinu.
bba	Mɑ bɑ mɑɑ ɡbee sinɑn sin weenɑsisu kuɑ wɔkurɑ yiru bɑ
bba	doke tiɑ tiɑ yɔɔtiɑ yen nɑɑ dɑbusɑru bɑɑteren yɛ̃si
bba	yɛ̃sikɑɔ. Nɔɔbɑ tiɑ yɑ wɑ̃ɑ nɔm dwɑrɔ, nɔɔbɑ
bba	tiɑ mɑɑ wɑ̃ɑ nɔm ɡeuɔ. Sunɔ ɡoo mɑɑ sɑri wi bɑ
bba	mɑɑ kitɑ ten bweseru kuɑre.
bba	Sɑ ǹ mɑɑ bɔnu ɡɑɑ mɔ kɑ wi.
bba	Roboɑmu u Abiɑ, Mɑɑkɑn bii yerumɑru wɛ̃. Mɑ u nùn kuɑ
bba	win mɑɑbu kɑ win wɔnɔbun ɡuro ɡuro. Domi u kĩ u nùn ko
bba	Yerɑ Yeroboɑmu u derɑ win tɔn be bɑ kukuɑ Yudɑbɑn biruɔ
bba	bɑ yɑrimɑ bɑ Yudɑ be wɔri. N deemɑ Yeroboɑmun tɑbu
bba	kowobu ɡɑbu bɑ wɑ̃ɑ Yudɑbɑn wuswɑɑɔ. Nɡe mɛyɑ n
bba	Wɑɑti ye sɔɔ, be bɑ dumɔ kɑ be bɑ yɑrimɔ bɑ ǹ bɔri
bba	yɛndu mɔ. Domi tɑbu wɑ̃ɑwɑ tem kpuro sɔɔ.
bba	Yinni Gusunɔ u kɑ Yosɑfɑti wɑ̃ɑ. Domi u sĩɑ Dɑfidi win
bba	sikɑdon yiri ɡbiikii sɔɔ. U ǹ bũu wi bɑ mɔ̀ Bɑɑli
bba	Sɔmɔ wi bɑ ɡɔrɑ u bu Misee sokuɑ u Misee sɔ̃ɔwɑ u
bba	nɛɛ, wee Gusunɔn sɔmɔ be bɑ wɑ̃ɑ mi kpuro bɑ sinɑ
bba	boko ɡɑri dori ɡeruɑ. Yen sɔ̃, ɑ de wunɛ kɑ ben ɡɑri
bba	Mɑ Yehu, Gusunɔn sɔmɔ Hɑnɑnin bii u nùn sennɔ dɑ. Mɑ u
bba	Yosɑfɑti sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, bɑ rɑ tɔn kɔ̃so somi? A be
bba	bɑ Gusunɔ tusɑ kĩ? Yenibɑn sɔ̃, Yinni Gusunɔ u kɑ nun
bba	Sɑnɑm mɛ Yudɑbɑ bɑ tunumɑ mìn di bɑ rɑ n tem mi
bba	ɡɑ̃ɑnu ku rɑ kpi wɛndɛ sɑ̃ɑ, yerɑ bɑ mɛɛrɑ berɑ
bba	mì ɡiɑ tɔn dɑbirɑ rɑɑ wɑ̃ɑ, mɑ bɑ deemɑ ɡonɑ nu
bba	Yerɑ Yinni Gusunɔ u Filisitibɑ seeyɑ kɑ Dɑɑrububɑ be bɑ
bba	wɑ̃ɑ Kusiɡibun bɔkuɔ. Mɑ bɑ Yorɑmu wɔri.
bba	Mɑ Yehoyɑdɑ u tɑbu sinɑm be yɑrɑ be bɑ sɑ̃ɑ tɑbu
bba	kowobu wunɔm wunɔm wiruɡibu. U bu sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, i
bba	Atɑli wi yɑro. Wi u mɑɑ nùn swĩi, kpɑ i yɛ̃ro ɡo kɑ
bba	tɑkobi. N deemɑ yɑ̃ku kowo Yehoyɑdɑ u rɑɑ bu sɔ̃ɔwɑ
bba	u nɛɛ, bu ku nùn ɡo sɑ̃ɑ yeru mi.
bba	Sinɑ boko Yoɑsi u duɑri ɡeɑ ye Sɑkɑrin tundo Yehoyɑdɑ u
bba	nùn kuɑ. Ye Sɑkɑri u ɡɔɔ dɔɔ, yerɑ u nɛɛ, Yinni
bba	Gusunɔ, ɑ wɑɑwo kpɑ ɑ bɑɑwure siriɑ.
bba	Mɑ Yoɑsi wi, u wurɑ kɑ sii ɡeesu ɡurɑ kɑ sɑ̃ɑ yerun
bba	ɡɑ̃ɑ ɡee ni nu wɑ̃ɑ Obɛdi Edɔmun yɛnuɔ kɑ sere
bba	mɑɑ sinɑ kpɑɑrun ɑrumɑni. Mɑ u ɡɑbu mɔɔru mwɛɛrɑ
bba	u kɑ ɡɔsirɑ win wuuɔ Sɑmɑriɔ.
bba	U wusu bɑnɑ Yudɑn ɡuunɔ. Mɑ u mɑɑ kɔ̃su mɑru yenu
bba	kuɑ kɑ dii bɑkɑ dɑmɡinu yɑkɑsɔ.
bba	Akɑsin kookoosun sukum ɡbiikisu kɑ dɑ̃ɑkisu si kpuro su
bba	yoruɑ Yudɑbɑ kɑ Isirelibɑn sinɑmbun fɑɑɡin tireru sɔɔ.
bba	Yerɑ Esekiɑsi kɑ Yudɑbɑn wiruɡibu bɑ Lefibɑ sɔ̃ɔwɑ
bba	bɑ nɛɛ, bu Yinni Gusunɔ siɑro kɑ Dɑfidin womusu kɑ mɑɑ
bba	Asɑfun womusu. Mɑ bɑ Yinni Gusunɔ kpunɑ bɑ nùn sɑ̃wɑ
bba	Domi Esekiɑsi u kɛtɛ kinɛnu nɔrɔbu (1.000) ɡɔsɑ kɑ
bba	yɑ̃ɑnu nɔrɔbun subɑ nɔɔbɑ yiru (7.000). Mɑ win sinɑ
bba	ɑsɑkpɔbu bɑ mɑɑ kɛtɛ kinɛnu nɔrɔbu ɡɔsɑ kɑ
bba	yɑ̃ɑnu nɔrɔbun subɑ wɔkuru (10.000). Mɑ yɑ̃ku kowobu
bba	bu tii dɑm kɛ̃ɛyɔ kpɑ bu wɔruɡɔru sɔ̃ɔsi. Bu ku
bba	bɛrum ko bu diiri Asirin sinɑ boko kɑ win tɔn dɑbi ten
bba	wuswɑɑɔ. Domi be bɑ kɑ bu wɑ̃ɑ bɑ dɑbi n kere be bɑ
bba	U wure u ɡunɡunu seeyɑ ni win tundo Esekiɑsi u kɔsukɑ. Mɑ
bba	u bũu wi bɑ mɔ̀ Bɑɑlin yɑ̃ku yenu kuɑ kɑ bũu wi bɑ
bba	mɔ̀ Asitɑɑten bwɑ̃ɑrokunu ni win tundo u rɑɑ kɔsukɑ.
bba	Mɑ u kperi kɑ sɔ̃ɔ kɑ surun sɑ̃ɑru wɔri.
bba	Tɔn be kpuro bɑ dɑ yɑ̃ku kowo tɔnwero Hilikiyɑn mi. Mɑ
bba	bɑ nùn ɡobi wɛ̃ yi Lefibɑ bɑ rɑɑ mwɛɛrɑ Yinni
bba	Gusunɔn sɑ̃ɑ yerun sɔ̃ sɑɑ Mɑnɑsen tem di kɑ
bba	Efɑrɑimun tem di kɑ Yudɑbɑn min di kɑ Isirelibɑ kpuron
bba	min di kɑ Bɛnyɑmɛɛn tem di kɑ sere Yerusɑlɛmuɡibun min
bba	Bɛɛyɑ i ko i Gɔɔ sɑrɑribun yɑ̃ku yɛɛ sɑkiri. Yen
bba	sɔ̃, i de i tii dɛɛrɑsiɑ, kpɑ i ten sɔɔru ko bɛɛn
bba	mɛro bisibun sɔ̃ nɡe mɛ Yinni Gusunɔ u Mɔwisi woodɑ
bba	Sedesiɑsi u mɔwɑ wɔ̃ɔ yɛndɑ tiɑ sɑnɑm mɛ u bɑndu di
bba	Yudɑɔ. Mɑ u kuɑ wɔ̃ɔ wɔkurɑ tiɑ bɑn te sɔɔ
bba	Sɑtun bweseru sɔɔ, bɑ sɑ̃ɑwɑ tɔmbu nɛnɛ kɑ wunɔbu
bba	Hɑrimun bibu bɑ sɑ̃ɑwɑ tɔmbu nɔrɔbu kɑ wɔkurɑ
bba	Yɑ̃ku kowo Yosue, Yosɑdɑkin bii kɑ win yɑ̃ku kowosibu kɑ
bba	Sorobɑbɛli, Seɑlitiɛlin bii kɑ win mɛro bisibu bɑ Yinni
bba	Gusunɔn yɑ̃ku yeru bɑnɑ seewɑ bu kɑ yɑ̃ku dɔ̃ɔ
bba	mwɑɑrɑruɡinu ko mi nɡe mɛ bɑ yoruɑ Gusunɔn woodɑn
bba	tireru sɔɔ te win sɔm kowo Mɔwisi u yoruɑ.
bba	I ku ɡɑri yi ɑtɑfiiru ko kpɑ kɔ̃sɑ yu ku rɑɑ sosi yu
bba	Gusunɔ wi u rɑ tii sɔ̃ɔsi Yerusɑlɛmuɔ, u sinɑ boko ǹ
bba	kun mɛ bwese te tɑ kĩ tu sɑ̃ɑ yee te surɑ kɑm koosio,
bba	yèn sɔ̃ tɑ nɛn woodɑ ɡɛmɑ. Nɛ Dɑrusiwɑ nɑ woodɑ
bba	yeni wɛ̃. I ye mɛm nɔɔwɔ mɑm mɑm.
bba	Yen biru, ɡoo ù n yinɑ u woodɑ ye mɛm nɔɔwɑ mɑm mɑm
bba	ǹ kun mɛ nɛ sinɑ bokoɡiɑ, bu yɛ̃ro sirio. Ǹ n ɡɔɔn
bba	nɑ u kɑ weenɛ, bu nùn ɡoowo. Bɑ̀ n koo nùn yɑrɑn nɑ
bba	ben suunu sɔɔn di, bu nùn yɑro. Bɑ̀ n koo nùn ɡɑ̃ɑnu
bba	mwɑɑrin nɑ, bu nùn mwɑɑrio. Bɑ̀ n koo mɑɑ nùn
bba	pirisɔm doken nɑ, bu nùn dokeo.
bba	Yen biru, nɑ bu sɔ̃ɔwɑ nɑ nɛɛ, nɡe mɛ bɑ wɑ̃ɑ
bba	nɛnɛm Yinni Gusunɔn sɔ̃, nɡe mɛyɑ yɑ̃ɑ ni, nu mɑɑ
bba	wɑ̃ɑ nɛnɛm Yinni Gusunɔn sɔ̃. Sii ɡee si, kɑ wurɑ ye,
bba	yɑ sɑ̃ɑwɑ kɛ̃ɛ ni bɑ Gusunɔ ben bɑɑbɑbɑn Yinni
bba	Wi u yinɑ u nɑ sɔ̃ɔ itɑn bɑɑ sɔɔ, bɑ koo win ye u mɔ
bba	wɔrɑ kpɑ bu nùn yɑrɑ Isirelibɑn suunu sɔɔn di. Woodɑ
bba	yeniwɑ Isirelibɑn wiruɡibu kɑ ben bukurobu bɑ yi.
bba	kɑ Bɑni kɑ Binui kɑ Simɛi
bba	Mɑ u tɑbu sinɑmbu kɑ mɑɑsɔbu ɡɔsɑ bu kɑ mɑn
bba	yɔ̃siri. Yerɑ nɑ seewɑ nɑ dɑ nɑ tem yɛ̃ro be deemɑ be
bba	bɑ wɑ̃ɑ sɔ̃ɔ duu yeru ɡiɑ mi. Mɑ nɑ bu sinɑ bokon
bba	Ben bɔkuɔ Esɛɛ, Yosuen bii, Misipɑn sunɔ u mɑɑ suɑ min
bba	di u kɑ dɑ sere mi bɑ rɑ tɑbu yɑ̃nu bere ɡbɑ̃rɑrun
bba	Yen biru, bɛsɛn yibɛrɛbɑ bɑ nuɑ mɑ bɑ sun sɔ̃ɔwɑ ye
bba	bɑ mɔ̀ kpuro. Gusunɔ u mɑɑ ben himbɑbɑ kɑm koosiɑ. Mɑ
bba	bɑɑwure u wurɑ mi u rɑɑ sɔmburu mɔ̀.
bba	Yinni Gusunɔ, ɑ mɑn yɑɑyo ye nɑ tɔn be kuɑn sɔ̃, kpɑ
bba	Pɑkɑti Mɔɑbun bweseru sɔɔ, bɑ sɑ̃ɑwɑ tɔmbu nɔrɔbun
bba	subɑ yiru kɑ nɛnɛ kɑ wɔkurɑ nɔɔbu kɑ itɑ (2.818). Bɑ
bba	sɑ̃ɑwɑ Yosue kɑ Yoɑbun sikɑdominu.
bba	Hɑrimun yɛnuɡibu bɑ sɑ̃ɑwɑ tɔmbu nɔrɔbu kɑ wɔkurɑ
bba	Wɔ̃ɔn suru nɔɔbɑ yirusen tɔ̃ɔ ɡbiikiru sɔɔ,
bba	Isirelibɑ kpuro bɑ wɑ̃ɑ ben wusɔ.
bba	Wunɑ ɑ hunde koni kpuro wɑ̃ɑru wɛ̃.
bba	mɑ ɑ kɑ bu ɡɑri kuɑ Sinɑin ɡuurɔ.
bba	Guru wii wuro te tɑ bu swɑɑ ɡbiiye mi,
bba	be bɑ bu kirɔ kuɑ bu kɑ ɡɔ̃ru ɡɔsiɑ
bba	domi ɑ sɑ̃ɑwɑ Yinni wɔnwɔnduɡii kɑ duromɡii.
bba	kɑ Hɑtusi kɑ Sebɑniɑ kɑ Mɑluku
bba	Mɛyɑ sɑ Gusunɔ nɔɔ mwɛɛru kuɑ sɑ nɛɛ, sɑ ko n dɑ
bba	kɑ bɛsɛn ɡberun dĩɑ ɡbiikinu kɑ bɛsɛn dɑ̃ɑ mɑrum
bba	ɡbiikum be bɑ sɔmburu mɔ̀ yɑ̃ku yerɔ nɑɑwɛ Yinni
bba	kɑ Sɑnɔɑ kɑ Adulɑmu kɑ yen bɑru kpɑɑnu kɑ Lɑkisi kɑ
bba	yen bɑru kpɑɑnu kɑ Asekɑ kɑ yen bɑru kpɑɑnu. Bɑ
bba	sinɑwɑ Beri Sebɑn di n kɑ dɑ Hinɔmun wɔwɑɔ.
bba	Be bɑ mɑɑ sɑ̃ɑ sɑ̃ɑ yerun kɔnnɔn kɔ̃sobu, berɑ
bba	Mɑtɑniɑ kɑ Bɑkibukiɑ kɑ Abudiɑsi kɑ Mɛsulɑmu kɑ
bba	Nɑ mɑɑ nuɑ mɑ bɑ ku rɑ Lefibɑ ben bɔnu wɛ̃. Mɑ Lefi
bba	be, kɑ wom kowo be bɑ koo sɑ̃ɑru ko mi, bɑ sɔmburu deri,
bba	ben bɑɑwure u dɑ u wɑ̃ɑ win temɔ.
bba	Adɑmɑ bɑ ǹ ɡoo tilɑsi kue u kɑ mu nɔ. Domi sinɑ boko u
bba	win sɔm kowobu sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, bu bɑɑwure derio u ko nɡe
bba	Asuresin bɑndun wɔ̃ɔ nɔɔbɑ yiruse sɔɔ, yen suru
bba	wɔkuruse wi bɑ mɔ̀ Tebɛsi, yerɑ bɑ kɑ Ɛsitɛɛ dɑ win
bba	Mɑ Hɑtɑki u dɑ u ye kpuro Ɛsitɛɛ sɔ̃ɔwɑ.
bba	Mɑ sinɑ boko u nɛɛ, u duumɑ.
bba	Yen sɔ̃ tɛ̃, i yoruo kɑ nɛn yĩsiru ye yɑ koo Yuubɑ
bba	ɑrufɑɑni kuɑ. Kpɑ i ye nɛ sinɑ bokon yĩreru koosi. Domi
bba	ye bɑ yoruɑ kɑ sinɑ bokon yĩsiru mɑ bɑ ye win yĩreru
bba	koosi, bɑ ǹ mɑɑ kpɛ̃ bu ye ɡɔsiɑ.
bba	Kpɑ bu kɛ̃nu mɔrisiɑnɑ. Kpɑ bu sɑ̃ɑrobu kɛ̃nu kɛ̃.
bba	Domi tɔ̃ɔ te sɔɔrɑ Yuubɑ bɑ ben yibɛrɛbɑ kɑmiɑ bɑ
bba	dɛrɑ. Suru wi sɔɔrɑ ben nuku sɑnkirɑnu nu ɡɔsiɑ nuku
bba	dobu. Mɑ ben nɔni swɑ̃ɑru tɑ kuɑ bɔri yɛndu.
bba	Sɑbeɡibu bɑ nɑ bɑ wunɛn yɑɑ sɑbe ni wɔri, bɑ
bba	mwɛɛrɑ. Mɑ bɑ wunɛn sɔm kowobu ɡo ɡo kɑ tɑkobi. Nɛ
bba	turowɑ nɑ kpĩɑ nɑ bu kisirɑri. Yen sɔ̃nɑ nɑ nɑ n nun
bba	Yen tɔ̃ɔ te, tu ko yɑm wɔ̃kuru mɑm mɑm.
bba	Nɛ, nɑ ɡɑbu wɑɑre, kɔ̃sɑn sɔmburɑ bɑ rɑ n mɔ̀,
bba	Nɡe Gusunɔn ɡɔrɑdo wɑrɑ kɑɑ soku kpɑ u nɑ u nun
bba	kpɑ u durumɡiin nɔɔ kɔre.
bba	Mɑ nin dɛ̃ɛ nɛn wɑsi duuri.
bba	Adɑmɑ bɑ̀ n turɑ mi, ben ɡɔmɑ rɑ dwiiyewɑ,
bba	mɑ yin kokosu wɔbirirɑmɔ.
bba	Sere dommɑ kɑɑ de n wɛ̃siɑ.
bba	yi rɑ ɡberewɑ fuuku n kere yɑkɑ si su tie.
bba	kpɑ mɛn ɡberebɑ bu wɔruku.
bba	Nɑ̀ n mɑɑ dɛɛren nɑ, nɑ ǹ mɑɑ wiru seeyɑmɔ, domi
bba	A tɑmɑɑ kɑɑ kpĩ ɑ Gusunɔn bwisikunu tubu?
bba	Ye u sɑnkɑ kpuro, ɡoo kun kpɛ̃ u ye sɔmɛ.
bba	Wɑrɑ u koo kɑ mɑn sikirinɑ nɛn ɡem sɔɔ.
bba	Kpɑ ɑ mɑn nɛn durum kpuro wɔkɑ.
bba	A win bwisi mwɑ kpuro, ɑ yi wunɛn tiin sɔ̃?
bba	ye yɑ nùn wɔriɔ nɡe sinɑ bokon tɑbu kowobu
bba	Mbɑn sɔ̃nɑ ɑ kɑ mɑn sikirinɑmɔ.
bba	Wi u sɑ̃ɑ ɡemɡii u koo yɔ̃rɑwɑ dim dim win swɑɑ sɔɔ.
bba	U ǹ mɑɑ sĩimɔ kɑ toro sindu.
bba	bu biti soorɑ win kɑm koo bin sɔ̃.
bba	Nɛn berusebu bɑ mɑn biru kisi,
bba	Adɑmɑ i n yɛ̃ mɑ Gusunɔ u koo bɛɛ siri.
bba	Ye u koo nɔ, yɑ ko n sɑ̃ɑwɑ nɡe wɑɑ dɛ̃ɛ,
bba	Kɑ mɛ, ɑ rɑ wɑ mi tɔn kɔ̃sobun yɑm bururɑm mu ɡbimɔ?
bba	Wɑrɑ u koo nùn win kɔ̃sɑ kɔsie.
bba	Kpɑ ɑ nùn nɑɑnɛ ko, ɑ nùn wunɛn wuswɑɑ sɔ̃ɔsi.
bba	Kɑ mɛ, u nɛn swɛɛ kpuro yɛ̃ yi nɑ swĩi.
bba	Adɑmɑ bɑ ǹ bekuru mɔ te bɑ koo wukiri wɔ̃kuru purɑn
bba	U ǹ mɑɑ dɔɔ win resɛm ɡbɑɑrɔ.
bba	Bilidɑ, wunɛn wisibu bu ǹ dɑm sɑriruɡii somimɔ.
bba	wi, wi u yinɑ u mɑn nɛn ɡem wɛ̃,
bba	ǹ kun mɛ nɡe kuu te kɔ̃so u kuɑ.
bba	Adɑmɑ tɔnu u kɑ̃kɑ u kperu wɔri u kɔsukɑ,
bba	U mɑɑ kpuro wɑɑmɔ ye yɑ wɑ̃ɑ tem sɔɔ.
bba	Domi nɑ rɑ wɔnwɔndo somi ù n somiru kɑnɑ,
bba	be, bèn bɑɑbɑbɑ bɑ ǹ turɑ
bba	nɛn bɛɛrɛ yɑ doonɑ nɡe woo.
bba	Nɡe mbɑ kon nùn sɔ̃ ù n mɑn sɛɛyɑsiɑmɔ.
bba	Nɑ ku rɑ yɛ̃ɛri wɑhɑlɑ yɑ̀ n nùn deemɑ.
bba	Tɛ̃, i de n mɑɑ ɡɑri ɡere kpɑ nɛn bwɛ̃rɑ yu kpunɑ.
bba	ɑdɑmɑ tɔnu u ku rɑ ye lɑɑkɑri ko.
bba	Yeni kpuron diyɑ Gusunɔ u rɑ kɑ tɔnu ɡɑri ko nɔn dɑbi
bba	U ku rɑ tɔnu nùn win ɡem bire.
bba	U rɑ bu sɛɛyɑsiewɑ nɡe tɔn kɔ̃sobu tɔmbu kpuron
bba	Nɛnɑ kon bɛɛ wisi wunɛ kɑ wunɛn bɔrɔ be.
bba	Kon nɛn yɛ̃ɛ bɑkɑru dendi
bba	kpɑ u de ɑ n bɔri yɛndu mɔ tɑ n kpɑ̃.
bba	Kɑ yebɑrɑ u rɑ kɑ tɔmbu siri.
bba	A yɛ̃ nɡe mɛ Gusunɔ u rɑ nu dendisinɛ,
bba	À n yen swɛɛ yɛ̃n nɑ, ɑ ǹ kɑɑ dɑ mi?
bba	Yɑ koo wurɑ yu kpunɑ wunɛn nɑɑ ɡɔ̃ɔwɔ?
bba	kpɑ yi n bɑllimɔ yin wɔllɔ.
bba	Gɑ koo nun suuru kɑnɑ ɡu nun ɡɑri dori sɔ̃,
bba	kpɑ ɡen nɔni yi n sɑ̃ɑ nɡe buruku sɔ̃ɔ yɑnɑ.
bba	Hɑnduniɑ yeni sɔɔ, ɡɑ̃ɑnu sɑri ni nu sɑ̃ɑ ɡen yinni.
bba	Wiyɑ u ku rɑ n wɑ̃ɑ kɑ be bɑ Gusunɔ ɑtɑfiiru mɔ̀.
bba	U nɛɛ, ɡisɔ nɑ kuɑ win bii.
bba	Nɑ̀ n yɑndɑ nɑ rɑ deemɛwɑ
bba	Nɑ rɑ n yɛ̃ɛrimɔ n kere be bɑ tɑm yibɑ.
bba	Kɑm kobɑ ben ɡere yɑ rɑ kɑ nɛ.
bba	Yibɛrɛbɑrɑ bɑ mɑn yeni kpuro koosiɑ.
bba	Yinni Gusunɔ, wunɑ kɑɑ tɔmbu siri.
bba	nɑ nun tɔmɑmɔ wunɛn kpɑ̃ɑrun sɔ̃
bba	Wunɛ wi ɑ sɔ̃ wunɛn sinɑ ɡɔnɑɔ,
bba	Nu ɡɑbu yinɑ bɛriɑ, mɑ nin tiin nɑɑsu wɔri ye sɔɔ.
bba	Kɔ̃sɑ ɡɑɑ kun bu deemɑmɔ.
bba	17-18 Yinni Gusunɔ, ɑ kɑnɑ nini swɑɑ dɑkio.
bba	bɑ rɑ wɑ ye bɑ kĩ ben nɔɔ dobun sɑɑbu,
bba	Nɑ nun nɑɑnɛ sɑ̃ɑ domi ɑ mɑn fɑɑbɑ kuɑ.
bba	Wunɑ nɑ rɑ n mɛɛrɑ bɑɑdommɑ.
bba	Tɛ̃, wunɑ nɑ soku, Yinni Gusunɔ.

bba	sɑriɑ ɡiɑ, kpɑ n wɑ ye n koorɑmɔ hɑnduniɑ ye sɔɔ,

bba	wɔ̃kuru, bɑ ǹ kpɛ̃ bu tubu ye Gusunɔ u mɔ̀ kpuro
bba	Bwisiɡiin ɡɑri yi rɑ n bɛɛrɛ mɔ. Adɑmɑ ɡɑri bɔkɔn
bba	ɡɑri yi rɑ ɡu kɑm koosiewɑ.
bba	Yen sɔ̃, su ɡɑri yi kpuron wii ɡoberu swɑɑ dɑki te tɑ
bba	nɛɛ, ɑ Gusunɔ nɑsio kpɑ ɑ win woodɑbɑ mɛm nɔɔwɑ.
bba	Yerɑ, n weenɛ bɑɑwure u ko.
bba	Wunɛn wĩirɑ kɑ ɡoonu wɑ̃.
bba	nɑ nɛn kĩnɑsin nɔɔ nɔɔmɔ.
bba	Ǹ n mɛn nɑ, kon sewɑ n bɔsu wuu sɔɔ,
bba	Nu mɑɑ nɔɔ nɛwɑ swɛɛ swɛɛ, nin ɡɑrɑ kun kɑnde.
bba	Wunɛ ɑ sɑ̃ɑwɑ nɡe dɑ̃ɑ ɡbɑɑrun dɔkɔ
bba	Nɑ nùn kɑsu kɑsu, nɑ ǹ nùn wɑ.
bba	mi turɑre bii wɑ̃ɑ yi yi kpiibu wee,
bba	Nɑ ǹ kɑ bɑɑru nɛn bwɛ̃rɑ mɑn suɑ,
bba	Mɛyɑ mɑɑ dɑɑnun nim yiburu tɑ ǹ kpɛ̃ tu kĩi te
bba	nɡe wuu ɡe bɑ tɑbu bure bɑ doonɑ.
bba	Bɑɑ ì n bɛɛn kɑnɑru dɛnyɑsiɑmɔ,
bba	mɛ Yinni Gusunɔ u sun wɛ̃ɛmɔ.
bba	ɡɑ̃ɑnu kpuro ɡesi ye bɑ kĩru bo.
bba	Yen sɔ̃, ɑ koowo bɛsɛn yɛnu yɛ̃ro,
bba	mɑ i ye i sɑ̃ɑrobu mwɑɑri yii bɛɛn yɛnusɔ.
bba	kpɑ ɑ de sɑ n wunɛn yĩsiru sɔɔwɑ.
bba	wɔllu kɑ tem Yinnin resɛm ɡbɑɑ te.
bba	Sɑɑ ye sɔɔ, tɔmbu kpurowɑ bɑ koo yiirɑ
bba	Yen sɔ̃nɑ Yinni Gusunɔ u koo de bu dɔ̃ɔ mwɑɑrɑ
bba	kpɑ wɔllu tu tĩrɑ ɡuru wii bɑkɑrun sɔ̃.
bba	Wee tɛ̃ win tii u koo bɛɛ yĩreru wɛ̃. Wɔndiɑ ɡoo u koo
bba	ɡurɑ suɑ kpɑ u bii tɔn durɔ mɑ, kpɑ u nùn yĩsiru kɛ̃
bba	Yinni Gusunɔ u mɑn sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, n seewo n yĩsi teni
bba	yore kpɑsɑsɑ, kpee bɛsi bɑkɑ ɡɑɑ sɔɔ, Mɑhɛɛ
bba	Sɑlɑli Hɑsibɑsi. Yen tubusiɑnɑ, bu seewo fuuku bu
bba	ɑrumɑni kpuro kɑtɑ ko bu ɡurɑ.

bba	Tɔmbu kpuro, Efɑrɑimubɑ kɑ Sɑmɑriɡibu,
bba	U koo bu nɔmu dokewɑ u sɛɛyɑsiɑ.

bba	Domi wunɑ ɑ sɑ̃ɑ bɛsɛn dɑm, wunɑ sɑ siɑrɑmɔ.

bba	Siriɡii be bɑ tie, bɑ ǹ Isirelibɑ bɛɛrɛ kerɑmɔ.

bba	Be bɑ sɑ̃ɑ tem mɛn dɑm bɑ koo kɔsikirɑ.

bba	nɑɑ swĩi bɑ mwɑɑmɑ bɑ yoo sɔmɑ koosiɑ kɑ tilɑsi.
bba	Nɑ bu nɛn sɔmɔbu ɡɔriɑmɑ sɑɑ yellun di, bu kɑ ben
bba	bɑɑwure sɔ̃ u win dɑɑ kɔ̃sɑ deri. Bu ku mɑɑ bũnu
bba	sɑ̃ kpɑ bu wɑ bɑ n wɑ̃ɑ tem mɛ sɔɔ, mɛ nɑ ben
bba	bɑɑbɑbɑ wɛ̃. Adɑmɑ bɑ ǹ sɔmɔ be swɑɑ dɑki, bu
bba	Yerɑ sinɑ boko u Yerɑmɛɛli wi u sɑ̃ɑ sunɔn bii, kɑ
bba	Serɑyɑ Asiriɛlin bii, kɑ Selemiɑ Abudɛlin bii woodɑ wɛ̃
bba	u nɛɛ, bu tire yoro Bɑruku kɑ Gusunɔn sɔmɔ Yeremi
bba	mwɑɑmɑ, ɑdɑmɑ Gusunɔ u bu beruɑ, bɑ ǹ bu wɑ.
bba	Yinni Gusunɔ u mɑɑ nɛɛ, u koo de Bɑbilonin tɑbu kowobu bu
bba	Yerɑ wiruɡii be kpuro bɑ nɑ Yeremin mi, bɑ nùn ɡɑri yi
bba	bikiɑ. Mɑ u bu wisɑ nɡe mɛ sinɑ boko u nùn sɔ̃ɔwɑ
bba	mɑm mɑm, mɑ bɑ nɔɔ mɑri bɑ yɑrɑ. Domi ɡɑri yi u nùn
bba	sɔ̃ɔwɑ mi, yi ǹ ɡinɑ yɑrɑ tɔɔwɔ.
bba	Yerɑ Gedɑliɑ u bu sɔ̃ɔwɑ kɑ bɔ̃ri u nɛɛ, i ku bɛrum
bba	ko i kɑ Bɑbiloniɡibu sɑ̃. I ɡesi sinɔ bɛsɛn tem mɛ
bba	sɔɔ kpɑ i Bɑbilonin sinɑ boko sɑ̃. Sɑɑ yerɑ i ko i n
bba	Mɑ bɑ Yeremi wisɑ bɑ nɛɛ, sɑ wurɑ su ko mɑm mɑm ye
bba	Yinni Gusunɔ u koo nun sɔ̃ su ko. Wiyɑ u koo ko bɛsɛn
bba	seedɑ dio ɡemɡii kɑ nɑɑnɛɡii sɑ̀ kun bɛsɛn nɔɔ
bba	Kon bu sɛɛyɑsiɑwɑ nɡe mɛ nɑ Yerusɑlɛmuɡibu
bba	sɛɛyɑsiɑ kɑ tɑbu, kɑ ɡɔ̃ɔru, kɑ mɑɑ bɑrɑnu.
bba	Gɑri yiniwɑ Yinni Gusunɔ u Yeremi sɔ̃ɔwɑ bwese tukunun
bba	kɑ sere Ludibɑ be bɑ sɑ̃ɑ tɛn towobu,
bba	bu Eɡibitin sunɔ yĩsi kpɑɑru kɛ̃ɛyɔ
bba	sere ɡoo kun kpɛ̃ u du mi,
bba	Tɔn be kpuro bɑ kuuki mɔ̀, bɑ weeweenu mɔ̀.
bba	domi wee bɑ nun tɑbu wɔrimɑm wee.
bba	Bɑ ǹ bu ɡɔsiɑre ɡɑm sɔɔ nɡe tɑm.
bba	kɑ Keriɔtu kɑ Botisirɑ, Mɔɑbubɑn wusu kpuro ɡesi, si su
bba	wɑ̃ɑ turuku kɑ tontondeɔ.
bba	I ɡɔɔ swĩiyɔ, Mɔɑbubɑ bɑ wɔrumɑ. Bɑ biruku yirɑ
bba	wurɑ. Annɑ ɑ sekuru wɑ. Be bɑ kɑ bu sikerenɛ kpuro, bɑ
bba	Rɑbɑ ye, yɑ koo bɑnsu ko,
bba	kɑ ben bekɑ kɑ ben sɔmunu kɑ ben yooyoosu,
bba	Adɑmɑ tɔ̃ru ɡɑrɑ wee tè sɔɔ kon de
bba	nɛ wi nɑ sɑ̃ɑ Isirelibɑn Yinni Dɛɛro.
bba	Domi tem mi, bũnɑ bɑ rɑ sɑ̃,
bba	Bɑbiloni kɑ yen tɔmbun sɔ̃.
bba	sere mu bu ɡo bɑ wiru biɑ.
bba	mɑ u wɔllu tɛriɑ kɑ win bwisi.
bba	kon wunɛ Bɑbiloni kɑ wunɛn tem tɔmbu kɔsie
bba	kpɑ bu ben yɛnusu dɔ̃ɔ doke.
bba	Domi bɑ Isirelibɑ dɑbinu ɡo.
bba	Ben hɑniɑ kpuro yɑ koo kɑm kowɑ dɔ̃ɔ sɔɔ.
bba	Nɛbusɑrɑdɑ sinɑ bokon kɔ̃sobun ɡuro ɡuro wi, u Serɑyɑ
bba	yɑ̃ku kowo tɔnwero mwɑ kɑ Sofoni wi u sɑ̃ɑ yɑ̃ku kowo
bba	Serɑyɑn yiruse kɑ sɑ̃ɑ yerun kɔnnɔn kɔ̃sobu itɑ,
bba	Yen yɑ̃ku kowobu bɑ weeweenu mɔ̀.
bba	Yinni Gusunɔ, ɑ nɛn nɔni swɑ̃ɑru mɛɛrio.
bba	kpɑ ɑ bu kuɑ nɡe mɛ ɑ mɑn kuɑ nɛn durum kpɑ̃ɑrun
bba	Mɑ wɔkinu nɔɔrɑ win sɑ̃ɑ yeru mi, nɡe tɔ̃ɔ bɑkɑnun
bba	Bɑ ǹ nun wunɛn torɑnu sɔ̃ɔsi
bba	Wee bukurobu kɑ bibun ɡonu nu kpĩ swɛɛ sɔɔ.
bba	mɑ u mɑn kuɑ nɡe yɑɑ ye u koo to.
bba	domi Yinni Gusunɔwɑ u nùn bu kpɛ̃ɛ.
bba	A duɑ ɡuru wiru sɔɔ ɑ ku kɑ bɛsɛn kɑnɑru nɔn sɔ̃.
bba	Yinni Gusunɔ, ɑ ben wɔmɑ nuɑ ye bɑ mɑn koosimɔ.
bba	kpɑ ben wuswɑɑ yɑ n bɑllimɔ nɡe kpee ɡobiɡinu.
bba	U ǹ ben yɑ̃ku kowo ɡoo doke ɡɑ̃ɑnu.
bba	mɑ sɑ nɔni yĩresu kokumɔ,
bba	Mɑ ɡɑ̃ɑnu tɛrie hunde koni ben wɔllɔ nu bɑllimɔ nɡe
bba	U turɑ Tɛli Abibuɔ, Kebɑrin dɑɑrun bɔkuɔ mi yoo be, bɑ
bba	wɑ̃ɑ. Mɑ u sinɑ kɑ biti bɑkɑ ben suunu sɔɔ sɔ̃ɔ
bba	Kpɑ ɑ sube teeru suɑ ɑ dɔ̃ɔ doke Yerusɑlɛmun suunu
bba	sɔɔ sɑnɑm mɛ yen tɑrusibun tɔ̃rɑ yibɑ. Yen biru kpɑ
bba	ɑ mɑɑ sube teeru suɑ ɑ n kɑ tu kɔ̃ɔ ɡe soomɔ ɑ kɑ
bba	wuu ɡe sikerenɑ. Yenibɑn biru kpɑ ɑ mɑɑ suberu itɑse
bba	suɑ ɑ pusi yɑm kpuro, yen biruwɑ kon bu tɑkobi suesi.
bba	wunɛ tɔnun bii, ɑ swɑɑ dɑkio ɑ nɔ ye nɑ ɡerumɔ bɛɛ
bba	Isirelibɑn sɔ̃. Nɑ nɛɛ, kpeerɑ wee. Tɑ pusi bɛɛn tem
bba	U duɑ mi. Ye u wɑ wee, yɛɛ yi yi rɑ kɑbiri kɑ yɛɛ
bba	kɔ̃si ɡɛɛn weenɑsii bɑ kuɑ ɡɑni sɔɔ bɑ kɑ
bba	sikerenɑ kɑ sere mɑɑ bũnu kpuro ni bɑ rɑ sɑ̃.
bba	Mɑ Esekiɛli u mɑɑ uruu nnɛ wɑ, yen bɑɑyere yɑ wɑ̃ɑ
bba	wɔllun kɔ̃so ben turon bɔkuɔ. Uruu yen bɑɑyere yɑ
bba	bɑllimɔwɑ nɡe kpee ɡobiɡiru.
bba	Mɛyɑ bɑ koo nɑ kpɑ bu bũu ni kpuro wunɑ ni bɑ rɑ rɑɑ
bba	sɑ̃ mi, ni nɛ, Yinni Gusunɔ nɑ ǹ kĩ.
bba	Domi nin ɡɑru sɑri te tɑ koo kɑm ko. Nɛn ɡɑri ɡɛɛ
bba	mɑɑ sɑri yi bɑ ɡeruɑ bu kɑ bu nɔni wɔ̃ke Isireliɔ.
bba	A bu sɔ̃ɔwɔ ɑ nɛɛ, ɑmɛniwɑ nɛ, Yinni Gusunɔ nɑ
bba	ɡeruɑ. Nɑ nɛɛ, Isireli ɡoo ù n tii wɛ̃ bũu sɑ̃ɑru
bba	sɔɔ, mɑ tɑ derɑ u torɑmɔ, mɑ u nɑ nɛn sɔmɔ ɡoon mi

bba	yɛ̃ro wisi nɡe mɛ̀n nɔɔ win bũnu dɑbiru nɛ.
bba	Goo kun wunɛn wɔnwɔndu kue u sere nun ɡɑ̃ɑ nin ɡɑɑ
bba	kuɑ. Adɑmɑ bɑ nun kɔ̃wɑ yɑkɑsɔ dɔmɑ te bɑ nun
bba	Wee ɑ derɑ bɑ wunɛn dukiɑ yɑrinɑsiɑ bɑɑmɑ, mɑ bɑ
bba	wunɛn tereru wɑ sɑnɑm mɛ ɑ sɑkɑrɑru mɔ̀ kɑ bũnu ni
bba	ɑ kĩ, ni nu kun mɑm wɑɑbu wɑ̃. Mɑ ɑ wunɛn bibun yɛm
bba	yɑri ɑ kɑ bũu ni yɑ̃kuru kuɑ.
bba	Mɑ tɑ dɑ̃ɑ ten kɑ̃ɑsɑ ye yɑ ɡunum bo wĩɑ tɑ kɑ
bba	dɑ tɑ yi tem mi bɑ rɑ tenkuru ko, wuu ɡè sɔɔ tenkubɑ
bba	U rɑ nɛn woodɑbɑ mɛm nɔɔwɛ mɑm mɑm. Tɔnu win bweserɑ
bba	nɛ, Yinni Gusunɔ nɑ rɑ soku ɡemɡii. Win wɑ̃ɑrɑ tɑ koo
bba	ye bɑ duurɑ dɑɑ torɑn bɔkuɔ.
bba	Yen sɔ̃nɑ ɡbɑburɔ nɑ nɔmu suɑ nɑ bɔ̃ruɑ nɑ nɛɛ,
bba	nɑ ǹ mɑɑ kɑ bu dɔɔ tem burɑm mɛ sɔɔ, mi tim kɑ bom
bba	mu kokumɔ mɛ nɑ bu nɔɔ mwɛɛru kuɑ.
bba	tɔnun bii, ɑ mɛɛrio sɔ̃ɔ yɛ̃sɑn nɔm dwɑrɔ, kpɑ ɑ
bba	bu ɡerusi be bɑ wɑ̃ɑ dɑ̃ɑ sɔ̃ɔ mi.

bba	tɔ̃nu kɑwɑ. Yen sɔ̃nɑ kon de bwese tukunu nu bu yɛ̃ɛ.
bba	Mɔɔn yĩsirɑ Oholɑ. Wɔnɔɡirɑ mɑɑ Oholibɑ. Oholɑ u
bba	sɑ̃ɑwɑ Sɑmɑri. Oholibɑ u mɑɑ sɑ̃ɑ Yerusɑlɛmu. Nɑ
bba	bu suɑ kurɔbu mɑ bɑ mɑn bii tɔn durɔbu kɑ tɔn kurɔbu
bba	Nɔrɑ ye, yɑ yɑsu, yɑ mɑɑ dɛ̃u.

bba	Wee ye Yinni Gusunɔ u ɡeruɑ. U nɛɛ, wee Filisitibɑ bɑ
bba	Isirelibɑ mɔru kɔsie kɑ dɑm domi bɑ sɑ̃ɑwɑ ben
bba	Esekiɛli u nɛɛ, Tiri, Yinni Gusunɔ u mɑn sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ,
bba	Toɡɑɑmɑɡibu bɑ rɑ mɑɑ dumi yi bɑ rɑ kɑ sɔmburu ko

bba	bu nun ɡɔɔ swĩiyɑ nuku sɑnkirɑnun sɔ̃.
bba	Win tenkurun kpɑ̃ɑru tɑ derɑ u bɔbunu kɑ keetɑ wɔri.
bba	Yen sɔ̃, kon nùn surɑ sɑɑ nɛn ɡuu dɛɛrɑ ten min di,
bba	wi, wi u sɑ̃ɑ nɡe wɔllun kɔ̃so mi. Kon de u doonɑ sɑɑ
bba	kpee ni nu bɑllimɔ min suunu sɔɔn di.
bba	Yen sɔ̃nɑ nɛ, Yinni Gusunɔ nɑ nɛɛ, kon Bɑbilonin sinɑ
bba	boko Eɡibitin dukiɑ kpuro wɛ̃. U koo ben yɑ̃nu ɡurɑ kpɑ
bba	nu n sɑ̃ɑ win tɑbu kowobun kɔsiɑru.
bba	Wee u sɑ̃ɑwɑ nɡe Libɑnin dɑ̃ɑ ye bɑ mɔ̀ sɛduru.
bba	Edɛnin ɡbɑɑ te sɔɔ, dɑ̃ɑ ɡɑɑ kun kɑ Eɡibitin sinɑ
bba	boko nɛ burɑm sɔɔ kɑ kpɑ̃ɑru sɔɔ. Kɑ mɛ, bɑ koo
bba	nùn surewɑ ɡɔribun wɑ̃ɑ yerɔ tem sɔɔ sɔɔwɔ kɑ
bba	dɑ̃ɑ ni nu wɑ̃ɑ Edɛni mi sɑnnu kpɑ u n kpĩ kɑ be bɑ

bba	sɔɔ. Yeniwɑ yɑ koo Eɡibitin sinɑ boko kɑ win tɔn dɑbi
bba	te kpuro deemɑ. Nɛ, Yinni Gusunɔwɑ nɑ yeni kpuro ɡeruɑ.
bba	Mɛsɛki kɑ Tubɑli bɑ kpĩ kɑ ben tɑbu kowobu kpuro. Mɑ
bba	tɑbu kowo ben sikɑ beɡiɑ sikerenɛ. Be, be bɑ ǹ Gusunɔ
bba	yɛ̃ mi, bɑ ɡuwɑ tɑbu sɔɔ. Beyɑ tɔmbɑ rɑɑ nɑsie.
bba	Yen sɔ̃, ɑ bu sɔ̃ɔwɔ ɑ nɛɛ, wee ye nɛ, Yinni Gusunɔ
bba	nɑ bu sɔ̃ɔmɔ. Nɑ nɛɛ, bɑ yɑɑ temmɔ kɑ yen yɛm
bba	sɑnnu. Bɑ bũnu sɑ̃ɑmɔ, mɑ bɑ tɔmbu ɡoomɔ. Yerɑ bɑ
bba	tɑmɑɑ tem mɛ, mu ko n sɑ̃ɑ beɡim?
bba	Kon nu kpɑro turo wɛ̃ wi u koo nu nɔɔri. U koo yɑriwɑ
bba	nɛn sɔm kowo Dɑfidin bweserun di. U koo nu nɔɔri kpɑ u n
bba	Sɑɑ ye sɔɔ, bɛɛ ɡuunun dɑ̃nu i ko kpɑrɑ kpɑ i binu
bba	mɑ win tɔmbu Isirelibɑn sɔ̃. Domi ben wurɑmɑru tɑ turuku
bba	Yinni Gusunɔn dɑm mu Esekiɛli nɛnuɑ mɑ mu win bwɛ̃rɑ
bba	suɑ mu kɑ dɑ wɔwɑ ɡɑɑn suunu sɔɔ. Wɔwɑ ye sɔɔ,
bba	wee ye nɛ, Yinni Gusunɔ nɑ ɡerumɔ. Nɑ nɛɛ, kon Gɔɡu
bba	wɔrimɑ wi u sɑ̃ɑ Mɛsɛki kɑ Tubɑlin kpɑro.
bba	Yen tɔ̃ɔ te, Isireliɔ kon Gɔɡu siku yeru wɛ̃ nim wɔ̃ku
bba	bɔruɡuun sɔ̃ɔ yɑri yeru ɡiɑ, mi tɔmbɑ rɑ sɑre. Kpɑ

bba	te sike, kpɑ bu yɑm mi soku Gɔɡun tɔn dɑbinun wɔwɑ.
bba	U mɑɑ dii sɔɔ ɡe yĩirɑ mɑ ɡɑ kuɑ ɡɔm soonu yɛndu.
bba	Dii ten berɑ ɡiɑ, sɑ̃ɑ yee ten yɑɑrɑ yɑ kɑ kɔnnɔ

bba	yɛ̃sɑn nɔm dwɑru ɡiɑ mi, tɑ sɑ̃ɑwɑ yɑ̃ku kowobun
bba	diru be bɑ rɑ sɑ̃ɑ yerun sɔmburu ko.

bba	sɔɔ. Mɑ bɑ kɔbɛ kuɑ ten tɔɔwɔ dii dɛɛrɑ ten

bba	Nɑ ǹ mɑɑ wurɑmɔ bu mɑn susi bu Isirelibɑ yɑ̃kuru

bba	dii te tɑ dɛɛre ɡem ɡem mi. Bɑ koo sekuru wɑ kpɑ bu ben
bba	Wee kɛ̃ɛ ni i ko i n dɑ wɛ̃. Ì n bɛɛn ɑlikɑmɑ kɑ

bba	kowobun sɔ̃ sɑ̃ɑ yerɔ. U duɑ sɑɑ kɔnnɔ ɡe ɡɑ
bba	wɑ̃ɑ sɔ̃ɔ yɛ̃sɑn nɔm ɡeu ɡiɑn di. Yen sɔɔ mi,
bba	ɑyeru ɡɑrɑ wɑ̃ɑ sɔ̃ɔ duu yeru ɡiɑ.

bba	nɛwɑ. Kpɑ bu yi kɔnnɔsu itɑ yɑbɑ nɡe mɛ bɑ yiɔnɔ
bba	kuɑ. Gbiikuu ɡɑ ko n Gɑdin yĩsiru mɔ, yiruse Asɛɛɡiru,
bba	Sinɑ boko u bu wisɑ u nɛɛ, nɑ yɛ̃ sɑ̃ɑ sɑ̃ɑ mɑ i
bba	kĩ i ɡɑri ɡɑwɑwɑ. Domi i nuɑ ye nɑ ɡɔ̃ru doke n
bba	Dɑniɛli u sinɑ boko sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, bwisiɡibu kɑ

bba	nun ɑsiri ye ɑ bikiɑ mini sɔ̃.

bba	kpɛ̃ɛyɔ dɔ̃ɔ boko wi bɑ sɔ̃ruɑ sɔɔ.
bba	Yerɑ dobo doboɡibu kɑ sɔrobu kɑ bũu sinɑmbu kɑ
bba	Bɑbilonin bwisiɡibu bɑ nɑ. Nɑ bu dosu ɡe sɔ̃ɔwɑ,
bba	ɑdɑmɑ bɑ kpɑnɑ bu mɑn ɡu tubusiɑ.
bba	Woodɑ ye, yɑ weewɑ sɑɑ Gusunɔn ɡɔrɑdobɑn min di kpɑ
bba	tɔmbu kpuro bu kɑ ɡiɑ mɑ Wɔrukoowɑ u bɑnnu kpuro nɛni.
bba	Wi u kĩwɑ u rɑ nu wɛ̃. U rɑ wi bɑ ǹ mɑm ɡɑrisi
bba	Sinɑ bokon mɛro u sunɔ kɑ win sinɑ ɑsɑkpɔbun ɡɑri yi
bba	nuɑ. Yerɑ u duɑ mi bɑ mɛnnɛ bɑ tɔ̃ɔ bɑkɑru dimɔ. U
bba	nɛɛ, sinɑ boko, wunɛn hunde yu dɑkɑɑ dɑ! A ku nɑndɑ
bba	sere wunɛn wuswɑɑ yɑ n burisinɛ.
bba	Sɑɑ ye Dɑniɛli u nuɑ mɑ bɑ woodɑ ye nɔmɑ doke, yerɑ u
bba	dɑ win ɡidɑmbisɑn wɔllɔ u duɑ yen dii sɔɔwɔ ɡèn
bba	fɛnɛnti yɑ wukiɑre Yerusɑlɛmun berɑ ɡiɑ. Miyɑ u yiirɑ
bba	u kɑnɑru kuɑ u Gusunɔ siɑrɑ nɡe mɛ u rɑ ko tɔ̃ru
bba	Yen biru, nɑ itɑse wɑ yɑ kɑ musuku ɡbeeku weenɛ mɑ yɑ
bba	kɑsɑ nnɛ mɔ yen biru wɔllɔ. Mɑ yɑ winu nnɛ mɔ. Bɑ ye
bba	yiiko wɛ̃ yu kɑ bɑndu di.
bba	Sɑɑ kɔbi yin tiɑn di, kɔbu piibu ɡɑɡɑ yɑrɑ ɡɑ
bba	kpɛ̃ɑ sɔ̃ɔ yɛ̃sɑn nɔm dwɑru ɡiɑ kɑ sɔ̃ɔ yɑri
bba	yeru ɡiɑ kɑ sere tem mɛ mu ɡeɑ bo ɡiɑ.

bba	bɛsɛ kɑ bɛsɛn wiruɡibu kuɑ. A derɑ Yerusɑlɛmu yɑ
bba	nɔni swɑ̃ɑru wɑ tèn bweseru bɑ ǹ wɑɑre ɡɑm.
bba	Nɛ wi nɑ sɑ̃ɑ wunɛn sɔm kowo, ɑmɔnɑ kon kɑ kpĩ n kɑ
bba	nun ɡɑri ko. Domi nɑ ǹ dɑm ɡɑm mɔ.
bba	Sinɑmbu yiru ye, bɑ koo kɑsu bu kɔ̃sɑ ko, kpɑ mi bɑ
bba	dimɔ mi, bu weesu kuɑnɑ. Adɑmɑ yen ɡɑɑ kun dimɔ. Domi
bba	kɑm koo bi, bu koo nɑwɑ sɑɑ ye bɑ yi mi, yɑ̀ n turɑ.
bba	Adɑmɑ wunɛ Dɑniɛli, ɑ de ɑ tɛmɑnɑ sere kɑ nɔrɔ.
bba	Sɑɑ ye sɔɔrɑ kɑɑ wɛ̃rɑ kpɑ ɑ se ɑ wunɛn ɑre mwɑ
bba	Mi bɑ ku rɑ rɑɑ bu soku nɛn tɔmbu,
bba	domi nɑ rɑɑ nuku dobu mɔ win mi n kere tɛ̃.

bba	I dɑm dɔrenɑmɔ, mɑ tɔn ɡoberɑ sosimɔ tɑ dɔɔ.
bba	kpɑ bɑ n turɑre dɔ̃ɔ dokemɔ ɡunɡunu wɔllɔ
bba	Mɑ Isirelibɑ bɑ ɡɔrɑ Asiriɔ
bba	Domi wɔnwɔndɑ nɑ kĩ, n ǹ mɔ yɑ̃kuru.

bba	Bɑ koo kowɑ yɑɑyɑɑre kowobu bwesenun suunu sɔɔ.
bba	Bɑ koo ben bũu yenu kpuro kɔsuku mi bɑ torɑ.
bba	Mɑ nɑ tu yɑrɑmɑ Eɡibitin di nɑ tu sokɑ nɛn bii.
bba	Nɑ sɑ̃ɑwɑ Dɛɛro bɛɛn suunu sɔɔ.
bba	Bɛɛ Isirelibɑ, i de i wurɑmɑ nɛ bɛɛn Yinnin mi.
bba	Wee sere kɑ tɛ̃, bɑ durum mɔ̀ bɑ dɔɔ.

bba	Bu wurɑmɑ win mi bu kɑnɑ teni ko
bba	Domi Yinni Gusunɔn swɛɛ yi sɑ̃ɑwɑ dee dee.
bba	Bɑ ku rɑ mɑɑ kɑ kɛ̃nu de Yinni Gusunɔn sɑ̃ɑ yerɔ
bba	Nɛ bɑɑsi, Yinni ɡoo mɑɑ sɑri.

bba	Kpɑ Yudɑbɑ kɑ Yerusɑlɛmuɡibu bɑ n wɑ̃ɑ ben temɔ
bba	Fenisibɑn torɑnu nu kpɛ̃ɑ.

bba	Mɛyɑ nɑ bɛɛ yɑrɑmɑ Eɡibitin tem di.
bba	Gunɔ ɡɑ koo tɑɑ mwɑɑrɑ temɔ
bba	i bu sɔ̃ ye nɛ Gusunɔ wɔllu kɑ tem Yinni nɑ ɡeruɑ.
bba	Nɛ, Yinni Gusunɔwɑ nɑ yeni ɡeruɑ.
bba	Nɑ rɑ nɛn bwisikunu tɔnu ɡiɑsie.
bba	Kpɑ u de bu ben wusun ɡbɑ̃rɑnu kɔsuku.
bba	Bɔ̃rurobɑ bɛɛ be i Yinni Gusunɔn siribun tɔ̃ru mɑrɑ.
bba	Ben wuu si, su bɛɛ Isirelibɑ kɑ Yudɑbɑn wusu ɡeɑ turɑ?
bba	Sɑnɑm mɛ yi tem min yɑkɑ si kpuro di, yerɑ nɑ nɛɛ,
bba	Yinni Gusunɔ, ɑ suuru koowo. Amɔnɑ Yɑkɔbun bweseru tɑ ko

bba	Nɑ nùn wisɑ nɑ nɛɛ, dɑ̃ɑ mɑrumɑ nɑ wɑ mɛ mu ye.
bba	Kpɑ bɛɛn bɑɑwure u sɑɑkibɑ doke u n wii pɔɔru pote

bba	Yonɑsi, ɑ seewo ɑ dɑ Ninifu wuu mɑro bɔkɔ ɡen mi. Kpɑ

bba	Kon bɛɛ mɛnnɑ nɡe yɑ̃ɑnu ɡɔ̃ɔ teu sɔɔ.
bba	Domi Yinni Gusunɔ u mɑn win Hunde wɛ̃.
bba	Goo kun mɑɑ nùn nɑndɑsiɑmɔ.
bba	U kĩ u bu mɛnnɑ nɡe ɑlikɑmɑ ye bɑ subɑ mi bɑ rɑ ye so.
bba	kpɑ bu sun wɔrɑ Asiriɡibu bɑ̀ n bɛsɛn tem wɔrimɑ.
bba	Bɛɛ Isirelibɑ, bɛɛ nɛn tɔmbu, kɔ̃sɑ mbɑ nɑ bɛɛ
bba	Tɛ̃, nɑ sɔɔru kpɑ n kɑ bɛɛ sɛ̃suku bɛɛn durum sɔ̃,

bba	Tɔmbu kpuro bu nɔɔ mɑrio win wuswɑɑɔ.
bba	Guunu nù n nun wɑ, nu rɑ diiriwɑ.
bba	Nɑ nuku dobu mɔ yèn sɔ̃ ɑ rɑ mɑn fɑɑbɑ ko.
bba	kɑ sere be bɑ ben sunɔn yɛnu dukiɑ yibiɑmɔ
bba	yen ɡɑɑ kun kpɛ̃ yu bu wɔrɑ Yinni Gusunɔn mɔru bɑkɑ

bba	sɔɔ. U seewɑ ɡɔrin di u ǹ wɑ̃ɑ mini. I mɛɛrio mi bɑ

bba	Ye bɑ wɑ̃ɑ mi, win sɑnɑm yibɑ ye u koo kɑ mɑ.

bba	nuku sɑnkirɑnu nu koo nun sɔku ɡɔ̃ruɔ nɡe tɑkobi.

bba	sɔ̃ɔsi, kpɑ i ku ɡere bɛɛn tii sɔɔ mɑ Aburɑhɑmuwɑ
bba	bɛɛn bɑɑbɑ. Domi nɑ bɛɛ sɔ̃ɔmɔ Gusunɔ u koo kpĩ u
bba	Aburɑhɑmu bibu seeyɑ sɑɑ kpee nini sɔɔn di.
bba	kɑ Enɔsi kɑ Sɛti kɑ Adɑmu kɑ Gusunɔ.

bba	ben ɡoo bɛkie, mɑ n kun mɔ Nɑmɑni Siriɡii.

bba	Yesu u bu bikiɑ u nɛɛ, i ǹ ɡɑrɑ tirerɔ ye Dɑfidi u
bba	kuɑ sɑnɑm mɛ ɡɔ̃ɔrɑ wi kɑ win bwɑ̃ɑbu mɔ̀?
bba	Goo ù n nun bɑɑ teeru so, ɑ mɑɑ nùn tensim tĩiyɔ, wi u

bba	Yen sisiru Yesu dɑ wuu ɡɑɡun mi, ɡe bɑ rɑ soku Nɑyini.
bba	Win bwɑ̃ɑbu kɑ mɑɑ tɔn wɔru ɡunɑ nùn swĩi.
bba	Mɑ Simɔɔ u nɛɛ, yinni, ɑ ɡeruo.

bba	Sɔ̃ɔ nɔɔbun biru, Anɑniɑ yɑ̃ku kowo tɔnwero u dɑ

bba	yɛ̃ro ɡoo wi bɑ mɔ̀ Terituru. Bɑ dɑ tem yɛ̃ron mi, mɑ
bba	Yen sɔ̃, i de su dɑ mi kɑ bɛɛn wiruɡibu ɡɑbu sɑnnu
bba	kpɑ bu ɡere torɑ te u kuɑ.
bba	Nɔɔ mwɛɛ teyɑ bɛsɛn bwesenu wɔkurɑ yiru nu kɑ Gusunɔ
bba	sɑ̃ɑmɔ ɡem kɑ tiɑ bururu kɑ yokɑ. Sinɑ boko, yĩiyɔ
bba	bin sɔ̃nɑ Yuubɑ bɑ mɑn mɛm mɑnimɔ.
bba	Miyɑ bɛsɛn tɑbu kowo tɔnwero u ɡoo nimkuu ɡɑɡu wɑ ɡe
bba	ɡɑ nɑ sɑɑ Alesɑndirin di ɡɑ dɔɔ Itɑli ɡiɑ, mɑ u
bba	Bɛsɛ be sɑ wɑ̃ɑ ɡoo nimkuu ɡe sɔɔ, bɛsɛn ɡeerɑ
bba	turɑ tɔnu ɡoobu kɑ wɑtɑ kɑ wɔkurɑ nɔɔbu kɑ tiɑ
bba	Bɑ ɡɑri yi sikirinɛmɔ, bɑ kɑ doonɑ. Adɑmɑ bu sere
bba	doonɑ Pɔlu u ɡɑri tee sosi win ɡɑri sɔɔ u nɛɛ,
bba	ɡeemɑ, Hunde Dɛɛro u bɛɛn sikɑdobɑ sɔ̃ɔwɑ sɑɑ
bba	Gusunɔn sɔmɔ Esɑin nɔɔ sɔɔn di,
bba	Nɑ wɑɑsun dibu nɛni wuu mɑrosuɡibun mi kɑ mɑɑ bɑru
bba	kpɑɑnuɡibun mi, yɛ̃ruɡibun mi kɑ mɑɑ yɛ̃ru
bba	Domi n ǹ mɔ be bɑ woodɑn ɡɑribu swɑɑ dɑki beyɑ bɑ
bba	ɡem mɔ Gusunɔn wuswɑɑɔ, mɑ n kun mɔ be bɑ mɔ̀ ye
bba	N ǹ mɛ tɔnɑ, sɑ mɑɑ nuku dobu mɔ Gusunɔ sɔɔ sɑɑ
bba	bɛsɛn Yinni Yesu Kirisin min di wi u derɑ sɑ dorɑ kɑ
bba	Domi sɑnɑm mɛ i rɑɑ sɑ̃ɑ torɑrun yobu, ɡem kun dɑm
bba	Domi Gusunɔn Hunden woodɑ ye yɑ wɑ̃ɑru wɛ̃ɛmɔ Kirisi
bba	Yesu sɔɔ yɑ sun yɑkiɑ sɑɑ torɑru kɑ ɡɔɔn nɔmɑn di.
bba	Wɑrɑ koo tɔmbu durum mɑni be Gusunɔ u ɡɔsɑ. Sɑri, domi
bba	Gusunɔn tiiwɑ u rɑ tɔnu ɡem wɛ̃.
bba	bɛsɛ be u sokɑ n ǹ mɔ Yuubɑn suunu sɔɔn di tɔnɑ, kɑ
bba	mɑɑ tɔn tukobun suunu sɔɔn di.
bba	ɑ̀ n kɑ wunɛn nɔɔ wurɑ mɑ Yesu sɑ̃ɑwɑ Yinni, mɑ ɑ
bba	nɑɑnɛ doke wunɛn ɡɔ̃ruɔ mɑ Gusunɔ u nùn seeyɑ
bba	A de ben nɔni yi wukiri bu ku kɑ wɑ.
bba	I bɑɑwure kɔsio ye n kɑ nùn weenɛ. I bu wɔ̃ɔ ɡobi
bba	kɔsio be n weenɛ i kɔsiɑ. I bu ɡbererun ɡobi kɔsio be n
bba	weenɛ i kɔsiɑ. I bu nɑsio be n weenɛ i nɑsiɑ. I bu
bba	bɛɛrɛ wɛ̃ɛyɔ be n weenɛ i bɛɛrɛ wɛ̃.
bba	N wɑ̃ ɑ ku yɑɑ tem kpɑ ɑ ku tɑm nɔ, kpɑ ɑ ku
bba	ɡɑ̃ɑnu ko ni nu koo kpĩ nu wunɛɡii torɑsiɑ.
bba	Yen sɔ̃, nɡe mɛ nɑ ɡbinnɛ kɑ Yesu Kirisi, n kɑ mɑn nɛ
bba	n tii siɑrɑ nɛn sɔmburun sɔ̃ te nɑ Gusunɔ kuɑmmɛ.
bba	I nɛn temɡii Herodio tɔbiri. I Nɑɑsisin yɛnuɡibu tɔbiri
bba	Nɡe mɛyɑ ɡoo kun kpɛ̃ u ɡere mɑ bɑ bɛɛ bɑtɛmu kuɑ
bba	Mɑ u sun ye sɔ̃ɔsi sɑɑ win Hunden min di. Domi Hunde wi, u
bba	rɑ n kpuro mɛɛrɑ u n kɑ yɛ̃, bɑɑ ye n wɑ̃ɑ Gusunɔn
bba	Pɔlu kɑ Apolo kɑ Sefɑ kɑ hɑnduniɑ kɑ wɑ̃ɑru kɑ
bba	ɡɔɔ kɑ ye n wɑ̃ɑ ɡisɔ kɑ ye n sisi siɑ, ye kpuro yɑ
bba	Nɑ bɛɛ tireru yoruɑ nɑ nɛɛ, i ku kɑ kurɔ dɑmɑ kowobu
bba	Adɑmɑ nɑ tɑntɑnɔbu kɑ ɡɔminibu sɔ̃ɔmɔ n ko n
bba	wɛ̃rɑ bɑ̀ n wɑ̃ɑ nɡe mɛ nɑ kɑ wɑ̃ɑ.
bba	Adɑmɑ nɛn lɑɑkɑri sɔɔ kurɔ wi, ù n tii deri ɡɔmini
bba	te sɔɔ win nuku dobu koo kpɛ̃ɑ n kere. Nɑ mɑɑ tɑmɑɑ
bba	Gusunɔn Hundewɑ mɑn yeni sɔ̃ɔwɑ.

bba	sɔ̃. Tilɑsiwɑ ye, yɑ mɑn sɑ̃ɑwɛ. Nɑ̀ kun yen wɑɑsu
bba	Aɑwo. Adɑmɑ nɑ ɡerumɔ mɑ ye bɑ kɑ yɑ̃kuru kuɑ,

bba	Gbiikɑɑ bɑ mɑn sɔ̃ɔwɑ mɑ, ì n mɛnnɛ, wuunu ɡɑnu
bba	wɑ̃ɑ bɛɛn suunu sɔɔ ni nu ǹ nɔɔ tiɑ sɑ̃ɑ. Nɑ mi
bba	Bɑɑ nɑɑsu sù n nɛɛ, su ǹ sɑ̃ɑ nɔmu, kɑ mɛ, su ǹ
bba	wɑ̃ɑ wɑsi sɔɔ? Su wɑ̃ɑwɑ wɑsi sɔɔ.
bba	Ǹ n mɛn nɑ, kĩrɑ n weenɛ i n kɑsu. I mɑɑ Hunden
bba	kɛ̃nu kɑsuo, n mɑm nɛɛre Gusunɔn ɡɑrin ɡerubun kɛ̃ru.
bba	Adɑmɑ ɡoo ù kun wɑ̃ɑ mi wi u koo kpĩ u ɡɑri yi tusiɑ,
bba	i de bu mɑri mɛnnɔ sɔɔ, kpɑ bu yi ko kɑ Gusunɔ tɔnɑ.
bba	Ǹ n wɑ̃ɑ teni tɔnɑn sɔ̃n nɑ sɑ Kirisi yĩiyɔ, sɑ
bba	sɑ̃ɑwɑ wɔnwɔndobu n tɔmbu kpuro kere.
bba	Nɛɡibu yeniwɑ nɑ ɡerumɔ, mɑ ye yɑ yɑɑ kɑ yɛm mɔ,
bba	yɑ ǹ kpɛ̃ yu bɔnu wɑ mi Gusunɔ u bɑndu swĩi. Ye yɑ
bba	mɑɑ sɑ̃ɑ ɡɔɔɡiɑ yɑ ǹ kpɛ̃ yɑ n wɑ̃ɑru te tɑ
bba	Nɛ Pɔlu, nɑ bɛɛ tɔburɑ kɑ nɛn tiin yorɑ.
bba	Yenin sɔ̃nɑ nɑ bɛɛ tireru yoruɑ nɡe mɛ nɑ kuɑ. Nɑ
bba	ǹ kĩ n turi bɛɛn mi kpɑ bu mɑn nuki sɑnku be n weenɛ bu

bba	nukuru tɑ̀ n dorɑ, bɛɛ kpuron nuku dobɑ.

bba	Hunde wɑ̃ɑ, miyɑ tii mɔrɑ rɑ n wɑ̃ɑ.
bba	Sɑ ǹ bɛsɛn tii ɡem wɛ̃ɛmɔ kpɑm bɛɛn mi. Sɑ bɛɛ
bba	ɑyeru wɛ̃ɛmɔwɑ i kɑ woo kɑnɑ bɛsɛn sɔ̃, kpɑ i kɑ

bba	ǹ kun mɛ, nɡe mɛ u nɔɔmɔ nɛn nɔɔn di.
bba	Nɛnɑ Pɔlu. Yesu Kirisiwɑ u mɑn sokɑ n kɑ ko win ɡɔro,

bba	Gɑbu be Yɑkɔbu u ɡɔrɑ mi, bu sere tunumɑ, Piɛɛ u rɑ
bba	rɑɑ di kɑ tɔn tuko nɑɑnɛ dokeobu sɑnnu. Adɑmɑ ye tɔn

bba	durum dɑm nɔmɑɔ, kpɑ kɛ̃ɛ tèn nɔɔ mwɛɛru Gusunɔ u

bba	I hɑniɑ koowo i n kɑ nɔɔ tiɑ sɑ̃ɑ ye yɑ wee Hunde
bba	Dɛɛron min di kpɑ i n ɡbinnɛ bɔri yɛndu sɔɔ.

bba	nɡe mɛ Gusunɔ u bɛɛ suuru kuɑ Kirisin sɔ̃.
bba	Mɛyɑ n weenɛ durɔbu bu ben kurɔbu kĩɑ nɡe mɛ bɑ ben
bba	tiin wɑsi kĩ. Wi u win kurɔ kĩ, u win tii kĩwɑ.
bba	Gusunɔ bɛsɛn Bɑɑbɑ kɑ Yinni Yesu Kirisi bu bɛɛ durom
bba	kuɑ kpɑ bu bɛɛ ɑlɑfiɑ kɛ̃.
bba	I ku ɡɑ̃ɑnu ko kinɛnun sɔ̃, ǹ kun mɛ tii suɑbun
bba	sɔ̃, ɑdɑmɑ i tii kɑwo kpɑ i wurɑ mɑ ɡɑbɑ bɛɛ kere.
bba	I n tii sɛ kɑ kɔ̃sɑn kowobu be bɑ sɑ̃ɑ nɡe bɔ̃nu,
bba	mɑ bɑ wɑsin bɑnɡo nɑɑnɛ sɑ̃ɑ.
bba	Nɑ yɑ̃ɑrun dɔɔnɛ mɔ, nɑ mɑɑ mɔɔ bɑkɑrun dɔɔnɛ
bba	mɔ. Yɑm kpuro kɑ ye n mɑn deemɑ kpuro sɔɔ, nɑ ɡiɑ mɛ
bba	kon ko deburun sɑɑ kɑ ɡɔ̃ɔrun sɑɑ. Nɑ mɑɑ yɛ̃ mɛ
bba	kon ko mɔɔ bɑkɑru sɔɔ kɑ yɑ̃ɑru sɔɔ.
bba	Bɛɛ mɑɑ, i rɑɑ ɡɑsɔ kɑ Gusunɔ tomɑ, i rɑɑ sɑ̃ɑ
bba	win yibɛrɛbɑ bɛɛn bwisikunu sɔɔ bɛɛn kookoo kɔ̃susun
bba	Geemɑ, woodɑ be, bɑ kɑ bwisin ɡɑ̃ɑnu weenɛ ɑ̀ n bu

bba	seserun serusiɑbu. Adɑmɑ bɑɑ woodɑ ben tiɑ kun dɑm ɡɑm
bba	mɔ yu kɑ wɑsin kĩru kɑnkɑm tɑɑre.

bba	ǹ mɔ su kɑ bɛɛ Gusunɔn Lɑbɑɑri ɡeɑ wɛ̃ tɔnɑ,
bba	ɑdɑmɑ kɑ mɑɑ bɛsɛn tiin wɑ̃ɑru, domi bɛɛn kĩrɑ

bba	I ku Gusunɔn sɔmɔbun ɡɑri ɡɛm.

bba	kuɑ kɑ nuku dobu, bɑ koo tɑɑrɛ suɑ.

bba	kɑ sere be bɑ ben tundobu ǹ kun mɛ ben mɛrobu ɡoomɔ, kɑ
bba	Domi tɔnu ù kun yɛ̃ mɛ u koo ko u kɑ win tiin yɛnu nɔmɑ
bba	sikerenɑ, ɑmɔnɑ yɛ̃ro wi, u koo kɑ kpĩ u Gusunɔn
bba	A ku hunden kɛ̃ru ɑtɑfiiru ko te tɑ wɑ̃ɑ wunɛ sɔɔ, te
bba	bɑ nun nɔmu bɛriɑ Gusunɔn sɔmɔbun ɡɑri sɔɔ sɑnɑm
bba	mɛ yiɡbɛ ɡuro ɡurobɑ nun nɔmɑ sɔndi wirɔ.

bba	u bɛsɛn Yinni Yesun Kirisin ɡɑri ɡemɡii nɛnɛ, kɑ mɑɑ
bba	sɔ̃ɔsi te tɑ Gusunɔn bɛɛrɛ wɛ̃ɛbu sɔ̃ɔsimɔ,
bba	A nɛn sɔ̃ɔsiru nɛnuɔ kɑ nɑɑnɛ dokebu Yesu Kirisi sɔɔ
bba	kɑ kĩi te ɑ mɔ win min di. Sɔ̃ɔsi te, tɑ sɑ̃ɑ ɡɑri
bba	Adɑmɑ ɑ tii ɡɑwo sɑɑ wiirɑ ɡɑri kɑ sikirinɔ yɛ̃ru
bba	sɑriruɡisun di. A yɛ̃ kɑm kɑm mɑ siyɑ su rɑ sɑnnɔ mɑ.
bba	Luku turowɑ kɑ mɑn wɑ̃ɑ mini. À n sisi ɑ de i nɑ kɑ
bba	Mɑɑku sɑnnu, domi u koo kpĩ u mɑn somi nɛn sɔmburu sɔɔ.
bba	kpɑ bɑ n tii yɛ̃ bɑ n sɑ̃ɑ tɔn dɛɛrobu kɑ tɔn
bba	ɡeobu be bɑ ben mɔrɑru nɔni doke, mɑ bɑ ben durɔbu wiru
bba	kpĩiyɑmmɛ, kpɑ ɡoo ku kpĩ u Gusunɔn ɡɑri ɡɑri kɑm
bba	Nɑ nùn kɑnɑmɔ u de nɔɔ tiɑ ye bɛsɛ kɑ wunɛ sɑ
bba	mɔɔsinɛ nɑɑnɛ dokebun sɔ̃ yu sɔ̃ɔsirɑ kookoosu sɔɔ
bba	kpɑ ɑ ɡɑ̃ɑ ɡeenu kpuro tubu ni sɑ mɔ Kirisin sɑɑbu.
bba	“Gusunɔn ɡɔrɑdobɑ kpuro bu yiiro bu nùn sɑ̃.”

bba	kɑ sɑnɑm mɛ bɑ win lɑɑkɑri mɛɛrɑ ɡbɑburu sɔɔ.
bba	i ku de bɛɛn ɡɔ̃rusu bɔbiɑ.”
bba	Ǹ n ben sɔ̃n nɑ, be bɑ rɑɑ yɑm wɑ Gusunɔn ɡɑri
bba	sɔɔ, mɑ bɑ win kɛ̃nu dendɑ, mɑ bɑ bɔnu wɑ Hunde
bba	Gɑri ɡɛɛ wee yi yi ye kpuro bururɑsiɑmɔ. Yɑ̃ku kowo
bba	tuko ɡoo yɑrɑ wi u sɑ̃ɑ nɡe Mɛɛkisidɛki.
bba	Bɑ ǹ kɑ nɛn ɑrukɑwɑni ye yɔ̃re ye nɑ kɑ bu bɔkuɑ.
bba	Geemɑ, nɔɔ mwɛɛ ten bweseru tɑ ǹ ɑrufɑɑni mɔ mɑ n
bba	kun mɔ wi u tu kuɑ u ɡu. Tɑ ǹ dɑm ɡɑm mɔ sɑɑ ye
bba	Hunde Dɛɛro u mɑɑ sun ye sɔ̃ɔmɔ. Gbiikɑɑ u nɛɛ,
bba	Kɑ nɑɑnɛ dokebɑ Isirelibɑ bɑ nim wɔ̃ku ɡe bɑ mɔ̀
bba	Nɑɑ yɑri tɔburɑ nɡe tem dirɑ. Adɑmɑ sɑnɑm mɛ
bba	Eɡibitiɡibɑ kĩɑ bu ko nɡe mɛ, bɑ nim diirɑ.
bba	I n tii sɛ kpɑ ɡoo u ku kɑ ɡoo kɔ̃ɔ mɛnnɑ tɑntɑnɑru
bba	sɔɔ, kpɑ ɡoo u ku mɑɑ yinɑ u ɡɑ̃ɑ dɛɛrɑnu bɛɛrɛ
bba	wɛ̃, nɡe Esɑu wi u bii yerumɑrun tubi dɔrɑ dĩɑ
bba	Ǹ n mɛn nɑ, sɑ n Gusunɔ siɑrɑmɔ sɑɑ Yesun min di
bba	kpeetim sɑri nɡe yɑ̃ku kobu, yerɑ sɑ n dɑ win yĩsiru
bba	Adɑmɑ i de i ko ɡɑri yin kowobu, n ǹ mɔ yin nɔwɔbu
bba	tɔnɑ be bɑ tii nɔni wɔ̃kumɔ.
bba	Nɡe mɛ wɑsi yi yi kun hunde mɔ ɡorɑ, nɡe mɛyɑ mɑɑ
bba	nɑɑnɛ doke bi bu kun sɔ̃ɔsire kookoosu sɔɔ, bu kuɑ kɑm.
bba	Gusunɔ turowɑ woodɑ wɛ̃ɛmɔ, wiyɑ mɑɑ sɑ̃ɑ siri
bba	kowo. Wi turowɑ koo kpĩ u fɑɑbɑ ko, wiyɑ koo mɑɑ kɑm
bba	koosiɑ. Ǹ n mɛn nɑ, wɑrɑ rɑ n wunɛ ɑ kɑ wunɛn winsim
bba	Yen sɔ̃nɑ i nuku doo bɑkɑbu mɔ, bɑɑ mɛ nuku sɑnkirɑnu
bba	nu kuɑ tilɑsi tɛ̃ sɑɑ fiiko sɔɔ, lɑɑkɑri mɛɛri
bba	Wi u tu nɑɑnɛ doke, u ǹ sekuru wɑsi.”
bba	Bɛɛ mɑɑ durɔbu, i n wɑ̃ɑsinɛ kɑ bɛɛn kurɔbu i n
bba	yɑɑye mɑ bɑ ǹ bɛɛ dɑm turɑ. I bu bɛɛrɛn kookoosu
bba	kuo, domi Gusunɔ u koo mɑɑ bu wɑ̃ɑru kɛ̃ kɑ bɛɛ
bba	sɑnnu. I n mɔ̀ mɛ kpɑ ɡɑ̃ɑnu ɡɑnu nu ku bɛɛn
bba	Bɛɛn bɑɑwure u de u kɑ win kɛ̃ɛ te Gusunɔ u nùn nɔmu
bba	sɔndiɑ dendi ɡɑbun sɔ̃ nɡe wi u kɑ Gusunɔn kɛ̃ɛ
bba	bwese bwesekɑ sɔmburu mɔ̀ dee dee.
bba	Yen sɔ̃, i kookɑri koowo i kɑ bɛɛn nɑɑnɛ dokebu sɔɔ
bba	lɑsɑbu ɡeɑ sosi, kpɑ i lɑsɑbu ɡeɑ sɔɔ yɛ̃ru sosi,
bba	Bɑ rɑ n sɑkɑrɑrun nɔni mɔ, torɑnu ku rɑ bu turi. Bɑ
bba	rɑ be bɑ kun yɔ̃ dim dim yinɑ mwɛ. Ben ɡɔ̃ru ɡɑ
bba	binɛn dɔɔnɛ mɔ. Gusunɔ u bu bɔ̃rusi.
bba	Sɑ̀ n nɛɛ, sɑ nɔɔ tiɑ sɑ̃ɑ kɑ wi, mɑ sɑ sĩimɔ
bba	yɑm wɔ̃kuru sɔɔ, sɑ weesu mɔ̀wɑ, sɑ ǹ mɑɑ ɡem
bba	Adɑmɑ bɛɛ, Hunde Dɛɛro wi i mwɑ Kirisin min di, u wɑ̃ɑ
bba	bɛɛ sɔɔ. Yen sɔ̃, i ǹ ɡoon bukɑtɑ mɔ wi u koo bɛɛ
bba	ɡɑ̃ɑnu keu koosiɑ. Adɑmɑ yèn sɔ̃ Hunde Dɛɛro wi, u
bba	bɛɛ ɡɑ̃ɑnu bɑɑnire keu koosiɑmɔ, ni nu sɑ̃ɑ ɡem, n
bba	ǹ mɔ weesu, yen sɔ̃, i n kɑ Kirisi mɑninɛ, nɡe mɛ
bba	Hunde Dɛɛro u bɛɛ sɔ̃ɔsi.
bba	Beni hɑnduniɑɡibɑ bɑ sɑ̃ɑ, yen sɔ̃nɑ bɑ kɑ
bba	hɑnduniɑn bwisi ɡɑri mɔ̀, mɑ hɑnduniɑɡibɑ bu swɑɑ
bba	Sɑ nɑɑnɛ sɑ̃ɑ mɑ sɑ̀ n nùn ɡɑ̃ɑnu kɑnɑ ni nu
bba	sɑ̃ɑ win kĩru, u sun swɑɑ dɑki.
bba	Nɛn kĩnɑsi ɑ ku kom kɔ̃sum sɑɑri mɑ n kun mɔ kom ɡem.
bba	Wi u ɡeɑ mɔ̀ u sɑ̃ɑwɑ Gusunɔɡii, ɑdɑmɑ wi u
bba	kɔ̃sɑ mɔ̀ u ǹ Gusunɔ yɛ̃wɑ.
bba	kpɑ bu nùn yĩsiru kɛ̃ Emɑnuɛli.”
bba	Mɑ Yosɛfu seewɑ u bii wi kɑ win mɛro suɑ bɑ kpɑm wurɑ
bba	kpɑ ɑ ku rɑ kɑ wunɛn nɑɑsu kperu sokurɑ.”
bba	Beyɑ bɑ koo tem mɛ tubi di.
bba	Adɑmɑ tɛ̃ nɑ bɛɛ sɔ̃ɔmɔ, bɑɑwure wi u win kurɔ
bba	yinɑ ɡɑ̃ɑnun sɔ̃ mɑ n kun mɔ sɑkɑrɑru, durɔ wiyɑ
bba	nùn sɑkɑrɑru koosiɑ ù n durɔ kpɑo suɑ. Durɔ wi u mɑɑ
bba	ɡoon kurɔ yinɑro suɑ, win tii u sɑkɑrɑru kuɑwɑ.
bba	A ku kɑ sun dɑ kɔkiribun berɑ ɡiɑ.
bba	Domi bɑɑwure wi u bikiɑmɔ bɑ koo nùn wɛ̃. Wi u kɑsu u
bba	koo wɑ. Wi u mɑɑ ɡɑmbo soomɔ bɑ koo yɛ̃ro kɛniɑ.
bba	Nɛn tii nɑ rɑ ɡɑbu wiru kpĩiyɛ, mɑ nɑ tɑbu kowobu mɔ
bba	be nɑ kpɑre. Nɑ̀ n turo sɔ̃ɔwɑ u doo, u rɑ n dɔɔwɑ.
bba	Nɑ̀ n ɡoo sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɑ, u rɑ n sisiwɑ. Nɑ̀ n mɑɑ
bba	nɛn yoo sɔ̃ɔwɑ u yeni koowo, u rɑ n mɔ̀wɑ.
bba	Mɑ woodɑ yɛ̃robu ɡɑbɑ bwisikɑ bɑ tii sɔ̃ɔwɑ bɑ
bba	nɛɛ, durɔ wini u Gusunɔ wɔmmɔwɑ.
bba	Sɑnɑm mɛyɑ Yesu ben nɔni bɑbɑ mɑ u nɛɛ, n bɛɛ kooro
bba	Bɑɑwure u koo bɛɛ tusi nɛn yĩsirun sɔ̃. Adɑmɑ wi u
bba	tɛmɑnɑ sere kɑ nɔrɔ u koo fɑɑbɑ wɑ.
bba	Kɑ ɡem nɑ bɛɛ sɔ̃ɔmɔ, be tɔn kurɔbɑ mɑrɑ sɔɔ
bba	ɡoo kun Yohɑnu Bɑtɛmu kowo kere. Adɑmɑ wi u yɑ̃kɑbu bo
bba	bɑn te Gusunɔ u swĩi sɔɔ u nùn kere.
bba	Tɔnu kun yɑ̃ɑru kere mi n tomɑ? Ǹ n mɛn nɑ, yɑ wɑ̃
bba	tɔnu u ɡeɑ ko tɔ̃ɔ wɛ̃rɑruɡiru sɔɔ.

bba	di ni nu beruɑ win ɡɔ̃ruɔ. Tɔn kɔ̃so mɑɑ ɡɑ̃ɑ
bba	kɔ̃sunu yɑrɑmɔ ɡɑ̃ɑ kɔ̃sunu sɔɔn di ni nu beruɑ
bba	I ko n mɛɛrimɔ ɑdɑmɑ i ǹ ko i wɑ.
bba	Setɑmwɑ mɑɑ sɑ̃ɑ yibɛrɛ wi u su duurɑ. Gɛ̃ɛbun
bba	sɑɑ mɑɑ sɑ̃ɑ hɑnduniɑn kpeeru. Gusunɔn ɡɔrɑdobɑrɑ
bba	bɑ mɑɑ sɑ̃ɑ ɡbɑɑ sɔm kowobu.
bba	Mɑ Yohɑnun bwɑ̃ɑbɑ nɑ bɑ win ɡoru suɑ bɑ sikuɑ mɑ
bba	Adɑmɑ bɛɛ i ɡerumɔ mɑ ɡoo ù n win tundo ǹ kun mɛ win
bba	mɛro sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, win dukiɑ ye u koo kpĩ u kɑ nùn
bba	Win bwɑ̃ɑbɑ nùn bikiɑ bɑ nɛɛ, mɑnɑ sɑ ko sere
bba	dĩɑnu wɑ ɡbɑburu sɔɔ mini ni nu koo tɔn dɑbi teni debu.
bba	Yen biru Yesu win bwɑ̃ɑbu sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, ɡoo ù n kĩ u

bba	tiin dɑ̃ɑ bunɑnɑru suɑ u n kɑ mɑn swĩi.
bba	Ye Piɛɛ u duɔ dirɔ Yesu ɡbiɑ u nùn bikiɑ u nɛɛ,
bba	ɑmɔnɑ ɑ wɑ Simɔɔ. Berɑ̀ n weenɛ bu hɑnduniɑ min
bba	sinɑmbu ɡbere ɡobi kɔsiɑ. Sinɑ bibu? Nɡe ɡɑbu.
bba	Ye sɔm kowo wi, u yɑrɑ min di, u kɑ win sɔm kowosi yinnɑ
bba	wi u win dibu nɛni nɡe fɔrɔtɔ nɔɔbun sɑkɑ. Yerɑ u nùn
bba	sɛ̃re u wĩiru sɛ̃kɑ u nɛɛ, ɑ nɛn dibu kɔsiɑmɑ bi ɑ
bba	Yerɑ Yesu u win bwɑ̃ɑbu sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, kɑ ɡeemɑ nɑ
bba	bɛɛ sɔ̃ɔmɔ, n sɛ̃ ɡem ɡem dukiɑɡii u kɑ bɑn te
bba	Yen biru u bu deri u doonɑ wuu min di u dɑ Betɑniɔ u kpunɑ
bba	“Kpee te bɑnɔbɑ yinɑ, terɑ tɑ kuɑ ɡɑni ɡɔmburun
bba	bɑ nɛɛ, tɔnwero, Mɔwisi nɛɛ, durɔ ɡoo ù n ɡu ù kun
bba	bii mɑrɑ, win wɔnɔwɑ koo win ɡɔmini yɛnu doke kpɑ u kɑ
bba	Bɑ mɑɑ sin yee bɛɛrɛɡinu kĩ dii yenu kɑ mɛnnɔ yenɔ.
bba	Mɑ Yesu u nɛɛ, Yerusɑlɛmu, Yerusɑlɛmu, wunɛ wi ɑ rɑ
bba	Gusunɔn sɔmɔbu ɡo kpɑ ɑ be u nun ɡɔriɑ kpenu kɑsuku.
bba	Nɔn nyewɑ nɑ kĩɑ n wunɛn tɔmbu kpɑɑsinɑ nɛn bɔkuɔ
bba	nɡe mɛ ɡoo mɛro ɡɑ rɑ ɡen binu mɛnnɛ ɡen kɑsɑ

bba	mii sɔ̃ɔ koo yɑm tĩrɑ, suru kun mɑɑ win yɑm bururɑm

bba	Lɑɑkɑriɡii be, bɑ wisɑ bɑ nɛɛ, ɑɑwo domi n ǹ koo
bba	bɛsɛ kpuro turi. I yɑnde doo i bɛɛɡim dwe.
bba	Sunɔ u koo bu wisi u nɛɛ, kɑ ɡeemɑ nɑ bɛɛ sɔ̃ɔmɔ,
bba	mɛn nɔ i bwɛ̃ɛbwɛ̃ɛ benin turo ye kuɑ nɛnɑ i kuɑ.
bba	Tɔnun Bii u koo ɡbi nɡe mɛ Gusunɔn ɡɑri yi win ɡɑri
bba	mɔ̀, ɑdɑmɑ nɔni swɑ̃ɑruɡiiwɑ wi u koo nùn dɔmɛ. N
bba	burɑm bo bɑ kun dɑɑ yɛ̃ro mɑrɑ.
bba	Yesun tɔmbun turo u win tɑkobi womɑ, u kɑ yɑ̃ku kowo
bba	tɔnweron yoon soo sɔ̃rɑ u burɑ.
bba	U nɛɛ, nɑ durum kuɑ ye nɑ kɑ tɔn dɛɛro ɡɔɔ bɔrie.
bba	Bɑ nùn yɑ̃ɑtɑm siriki mɑ bɑ dɛkɑ wɛ̃ɛnɑ bɑ kɑ
bba	Mɑɑri Mɑdɑlɑɡii kɑ Mɑɑri wiɔnɔ bɑ sɔ̃ siki ten
bba	Bɑɑ mɛ i ye kpuro yɛ̃ sɑ̃ɑ sɑ̃ɑ, kɑ mɛ, nɑ kĩ n
bba	bɛɛ yɑɑyɑsiɑ mɑ ye Yinni Gusunɔ u Isirelin tɔmbu wɔrɑ
bba	sɑɑ Eɡibitin tem di u kpɑ, yen biru u be bɑ ǹ nɑɑnɛ
bba	ɡɑ nɛɛ, n yoruo tireru sɔɔ ye nɑ wɑɑmɔ, kpɑ n tire te
bba	mɔrisiɑ Yesun yiɡbɛnu nɔɔbɑ yirun mi, Efesuɔ, kɑ
bba	Simiiniɔ, kɑ Pɛɛɡɑmuɔ, kɑ Tiɑtirɑɔ, kɑ Sɑɑduɔ,
bba	kɑ Filɑdɛɛfiɔ, kɑ Lodiseɔ.
bba	nɑ win kookoosu yɛ̃. Nɑ win kĩru yɛ̃, kɑ win
bba	bɔrɔkiniru, kɑ win tɔn ɡeeru kɑ mɑɑ win tɛmɑnɑbu. Nɑ
bba	yɛ̃ mɑ win sɔm dɑ̃ɑkiru tɑ ɡbiikiru kere.
bba	Wi u swɑɑ mɔ u nɔɔwɔ ye Hunde Dɛɛro u Yesun yiɡbɛnu
bba	Kperi mɑɑ wɔrukumɔ temɔ nɡe mɛ ɡɑndun bii birenu rɑ
bba	dɛrure sɑnɑm mɛ woo dɑmɡuu ɡɑ tu sirɑmɔ.
bba	mɑ hunde konibɑ kpuro be bɑ wɑ̃ɑ nim wɔ̃ku sɔɔn bɔnu
bba	itɑse bɑ ɡu, ɡoo nimkusu kpuron bɔnu itɑse yɑ mɑɑ kɑm
bba	mɑ u bɔ̃ruɑ kɑ Gusunɔn yĩsiru wi u wɑ̃ɑ sere kɑ
bba	bɑɑdommɑɔ, wi u wɔllu kɑ ten ɡɑ̃ɑnu tɑkɑ kuɑ, kɑ
bba	tem kɑ mɛn ɡɑ̃ɑnu kɑ mɑɑ nim wɔ̃ku kɑ ɡen
bba	ɡɑ̃ɑnu. Gɔrɑdo wi, u ɡeruɑ u nɛɛ, sɑɑ kun mɑɑ
bba	Sɑɑ yɑ turɑ bu kɑ ɡɔribu siri.
bba	Bɑ ye swɑɑ kɑ̃ yu kɑ nɑɑnɛ dokeobu tɑbu ko kpɑ yu bu
bba	tɑbu di. Bɑ mɑɑ ye yiiko wɛ̃ bweseru bɑɑteren wɔllɔ,
bba	kɑ tɔmbu kpuro kɑ bɑrum bɑɑmɛre kɑ tem bɑɑmɛre.
bba	Bɑ resɛm dɑ̃ɑ bii ni ɡɑmɑ nin ɡɑmɑ yerɔ wuun biruɔ.
bba	Mɑ dɑ̃ɑ bii ɡɑmɑ yee ten min di yɛm mu kokɑ mu tɛriɑ
bba	sere kilo ɡoobɑ wunɔbu (300), mɑ mɛn dukum mɑɑ turɑ sere
bba	Yerɑ wɛrɛku ni, nu sinɑmbu kpuro mɛnnɑ ɡɑm ɡum mi bɑ
bba	rɑ soku kɑ Heberum Aɑmɑɡedom.
bba	I ye tɔ̃yɑ kɑ nuku sɑnkirɑnu kɔsio, nɡe mɛ yɑ yen
bba	yiiko kɑ dukiɑn doo nɔɔru di. Domi yɑ yen tii sɔ̃ɔwɑ
bba	yɑ nɛɛ, wee, yɑ sɔ̃ nɡe sinɑ boko, yɑ ǹ sɑ̃ɑ
bba	ɡɔmini. Mɛyɑ yɑ ǹ mɑɑ nuku sɑnkirɑnu wɑsi pɑi.
bba	Nɑ mɑɑ wɑ Gusunɔ wɔllɑ wukiɑrɑ mɑ dum kɑɑ ɡɑɑ
bba	kurɑmɑ. Wi u ye sɔni win yĩsirɑ Gemɡii kɑ Bɔrɔkini. Gem
bba	sɔɔrɑ u rɑ siri, mɛyɑ u rɑ mɑɑ kɑ tɑbu ko.
bba	U mɑɑ mɑn sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, n yeni yoruo domi win ɡɑri,
bba	ɡɑri ɡeeyɑ, yi mɑɑ sɑ̃ɑ nɑɑnɛɡii.
bba	Nɛ Yohɑnu nɑ yɑbu yeni nuɑ, nɑ mɑɑ ye wɑ. Ye nɑ ye
bba	nuɑ nɑ ye wɑ nɑ kpɑ, nɑ kpunɑ wɔllun ɡɔrɑdo win
bba	wuswɑɑɔ wi u mɑn ye kpuro sɔ̃ɔsi, n kɑ nùn sɑ̃.
